40001001	Ȧkȧfȧ ka rȧkom ra Yisɔs Krayst ɔWan ka Debid , ɔwan ka Ebraham , ki ake .
40001002	Ebrahamȧŋ ɔ kom Aysakȧŋ , Aysak ɔ kom Yekɔbȧŋ , Yekɔb ɔ kom Yudasȧŋ yi aŋwɔnt ŋɔŋ aruni .
40001003	Yudasȧŋ ɔ kom Ferɛs yi Sara ka Temar ; Ferɛsȧŋ ɔ kom Hɛsrɔn ; ka Hɛsrɔnȧŋ ɔ kom Aram ;
40001004	Eramȧŋ ɔ kom Aminadab ; ka Aminadabȧŋ ɔ kom Nesɔn ; ka Nesɔnȧŋ ɔ kom Salmɔn ;
40001005	ɔwa Salmɔnȧŋ ɔ kom Bowas ka Rehab ; ka Bowasȧŋ ɔ kom Obɛd ka Ruth ; ka Obɛdȧŋ ɔ kom Yɛsi ;
40001006	Yɛsiȧŋ ɔ kom Debidȧŋ ɔbȧy ; ka Debid ɔbȧy ɔ kom Sɔlɔmɔn ka ɔrani ka Urayas ;
40001007	Sɔlɔmɔnȧŋ ɔ kom Rihoboam ; ka Rihoboamȧŋ ɔ kom Abaya ; ka Abayaŋ ɔ kom Asa ;
40001008	Asaŋ ɔ kom Yehosafat ; ka Yehosafatȧŋ ɔ kom Yoram ; ka Yoramȧŋ ɔ kom Osaya ;
40001009	ka Osayaŋ ɔ kom Yotham ; ka Yothamȧŋ ɔ kom Ehas ; ka Ehasȧŋ ɔ kom Hɛsikaya ;
40001010	ka Hɛsikayaŋ ɔ kom Manasɛ ; ka Manasɛŋ ɔ kom Emɔs ; ka Amanȧŋ ɔ kom Yosaya ;
40001011	ka Yosayaŋ ɔ kom Yɛkonaya , yi aŋwɔnt ŋɔŋ aruni ka ȧŋlɔkɔ a kera ŋa ro Babilɔn .
40001012	Kǝdarǝŋ ka ma a kera ŋa ro Babilɔn-e , Yɛkonayaŋ ɔ kom Salathiyɛl ; ka Salathiɛlȧŋ ɔ kom Sirɔbabɛl ;
40001013	ka Sirɔbabɛlȧŋ ɔ kom Abiud ; ka Abiudȧŋ ɔ kom Ilayakim ; ka Ilayakimȧŋ ɔ kom Asɔr ;
40001014	ka Asɔr ɔ kom Sedɔk ; ka Sedɔkȧŋ ɔ kom Akim ; ka Akimȧŋ ɔ kom Ilayud ;
40001015	ka Ilayudȧŋ ɔ kom Ɛliyesar ; ka Ɛliyesarȧŋ ɔ kom Mȧthan ; ka Mȧthanȧŋ ɔ kom Yekɔb ;
40001016	ka Yekɔbȧŋ ɔ kom Yosɛf ɔwos ka Meri ɔwe kom Yisɔsȧŋ , ɔwe a bont Krayst .
40001017	Ɔwa takomra bɛ kǝtǝp ka Ebraham haŋ ka Debid tǝ yi tǝkomra tɔfɔt tanlɛ ; ɔwa kǝtǝp ka Debid haŋ ka kakera ŋa ro Babilɔn tǝ yi tǝkomra tɔfɔt tanlɛ ; ɔwa kǝtǝp ka kakera ŋa ro Babilɔn haŋ ka Kraist-e , tǝ yi tǝkomra tɔfɔt tanlɛ .
40001018	Ɔwa kakom ka Yisɔs kǝ yi yaŋ ; ma Yosɛf ɔ po fath Meriȧŋ ɔkara ka Yisɔs , yeŋka aŋ yiranɛ-e , a fir kǝpa ɔ yi ukor ka ɔYina mǝsǝm .
40001019	Kɛrɛ Yosɛfȧŋ ɔwos kɔŋ-e , ma ɔ yi wuni lompi-e , ɔ yema hɛ wɔŋȧ kɔ mǝlap-e , ɔ nanɛ tǝ kǝter kɔ sɔy .
40001020	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ tȧmtȧmnɛ mȧtȧy ame-e , kǝla , ɔmaleka ka ɔMarki ɔ tɔrinɛ ro ŋɔŋ rǝ mǝrei , kɔ pa , Yosɛf , munɔ ɔwan ka Debid , te nesa tǝ kǝba ro mu Meriȧŋ , ɔrani ka mu-e , kotȧy-e ɔ yi ukor ka ɔYina mǝsǝm .
40001021	Ɔ tǝ kom wath uruni . Ɔwa mǝ yi tǝ kǝbont kɔ ŋes Yisɔs , kotȧy-e kɔnɔ mǝ kisis aŋfǝm ŋɔŋ ka ɛhakɛ yaŋ .
40001022	Ȧte bɛ tǝ yɔnɛ kȧmȧ ȧrim ra ɔMarki rǝ lasǝr ka tapa ta aŋnabi-e , kepa
40001023	Kǝla , ufanɛ ɔ tǝ gbasi kor , Ɔ tǝ kom wath uruni , Ɔwa a tǝ bont kɔ ŋes , Imanuɛl , ( aŋa a tepa kǝpa Kuruȧŋ ɔ yi dɛ yi saŋ ) .
40001024	Ɔwa ma Yosɛf ɔ thǝmɛ ka mȧrey mɔŋ-e , ɔ yɔ mɔ mǝ ɔmaleka ka ɔMarki ɔ yamari kɔ , kɔ gbasi ɔrani kɔŋ ro seth kɔŋ .
40001025	Kɛrɛ ɔ tɛ hɛ kɔ haŋ ɔ po kom ɔwan kɔŋ uruni utɔtɔkɔ . Ka a bont kɔ ŋes Yisɔs .
40002001	Ɔwa ma a kom Yisɔsȧŋ ro Bɛthlihɛm ȧke ro Yudia ka mȧrey ma Hɛrɔd ɔbay-e , kǝla , afǝm atempi aŋ der ro Yerusalɛm kǝyɛfȧ ro thɔrɔŋ ,
40002002	kaŋ pa , Kɔn-a ɔwe a kom ubȧy ka aŋYuda-a ? kotȧy-e sǝ po nənk akɔs kɔŋ ro thɔrɔŋ , ɔwa sǝ der tǝ kǝbatho kɔ .
40002003	Ma Herodȧŋ ɔbȧy ɔ tǝl ti-e , pǝ sɔmpa kɔ yi aŋfǝm bɛ ro Yerusalɛm .
40002004	kɔ thoŋkla aŋfode ȧbana yi aŋkarmɔkɔ ŋa aŋfǝme , ɔ yifǝth ŋa ta ro a yi tǝ kǝkom ɔKrayst .
40002005	kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Ro Bɛthlihɛm ȧke ka ȧŋthɔf ŋa ro Yudia ; kotȧy-e yaŋ ɔnȧbi ɔ gbal kǝpa ,
40002006	Munɔ Bɛthlihɛm , ka ȧŋthɔf ŋa Yuda , Mǝ yi hɛ ulɔl pǝthas aŋkərbomp ŋa aŋ Yuda ; kotȧy-e ugbǝkȧ ɔ tǝwur ro mu Ɔwe mǝ yi ɔbumǝr ka aŋfǝm a mi aŋIsrɛl .
40002007	Ka Herodȧŋ ɔ tela aŋfǝm atempi sɔy , kɔ yifǝth ŋa finɔ ta ȧŋlɔkɔ aŋa akɔs kǝ tɔrinɛ .
40002008	kɔ som ŋa ro Bɛthlihɛm , kɔ pa , Kɔnɛ nu , thɛns ɔfinɔ ta ɔwath . Bepi nǝ po fir kɔ-e , de nu tɔri mi , kȧmȧ minɛ sɔ i gbǝli kɔ bȧtho kɔ .
40002009	Maŋ po tǝla ɔbay-e , aŋ kɔnɛ ro Bɛthlihɛm , ka akɔs ȧke aŋ nənk ro thɔrɔŋ kǝ tǝma ŋa kǝdi haŋ kǝ re tǝma rokɔm ka ɔdɛr ro ɔwath ɔ yi .
40002010	Maŋ nənk akɔs-e , aŋ selanɛ mǝbɔnɛ mǝbana .
40002011	Maŋ po wɔŋ ka ȧŋseth-e , aŋ nənk ɔwath yi ɔkara kɔŋ Meriȧŋ , kaŋ gbǝpsa , aŋ bȧtho kɔ . Ɔwa maŋ po kanthi ɛbɛnɛnɛ yaŋ-e , aŋ sɔŋ kɔ ɛboya ; mǝbɔŋɔ-o , agboŋgbo-o yi aŋma .
40002012	Ɔwa , ma Kuruȧŋ ɔ maŋ ŋa rǝ mǝrei kȧmȧ aŋ te kȧlanɛ ka Herod-e , aŋ kȧlanɛ ka ȧŋthɔf ŋaŋ rǝ roŋ dǝlɔm .
40002013	Ɔwa maŋ po kɔnɛ-e , kǝla , umȧleka ka ɔMarki ɔ tɔrinɛ ka Yosɛf rǝ mǝrei , ɔ pa , Yokanɛ mǝ gbasi ɔwath yi ɔkara kɔŋ , mǝ gbukɛ mǝ kɔ ro Iyipt , kȧmȧ mǝ yi ri haŋ i kanɛ mu ; kotȧy-e Herodȧŋ ɔ tǝ thɛns tǝ kǝdif ɔwath .
40002014	kɔ yokanɛ , ɔ gbasi ɔwath yi ɔkara kɔŋ ka tȧtȧk , ɔ kɔnɛ ro Iyipt .
40002015	kɔ yi ri haŋ rafi ra Hɛrɔd ; kȧmȧ ȧrim ra ɔMarki rǝ lasǝr ara ɔ pa ka kasǝŋ ka ɔnȧbi , I po tela ɔwan kȧmi tǝ kǝwur ro Iyipt .
40002016	Herodȧŋ , ma ɔ nənk kǝpa aŋfǝm atempi aŋ po pǝŋis kɔ-e , ɔ bansȧ haŋ , kɔ som afǝm tǝ kǝdifǝth aŋfɛth aruni bɛ ro Bɛthlihɛm yi ka mȧgbȧp mati bɛ , aŋfɛth aŋa bȧk tǝren tǝrǝŋ yi aŋa te tha bekȧ yi-e , mɔ mǝ ȧŋlɔkɔ aŋ yi aŋa ɔ gbɛlɛŋ aŋfǝm atempi .
40002017	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati ȧrim ra Yɛrimaya ɔnȧbi rǝ lasǝr , ara pa ,
40002018	A tǝla rim ro Rama , Kǝbok yi rǝbora rǝbana . Retɛl ɔ bok ta aŋwuth ŋɔŋ ; Ɔ selɔ hɛ a thɔnthɔ kɔ , pǝkasifɛ aŋ yi hɛ sɔ .
40002019	Kɛrɛ ma Herodȧŋ ɔ fi-e , umalek ka ɔMarki ɔ tɔrinɛ ka Yosɛf ro Iyipt rǝ mǝrey ,
40002020	kɔ pa , Yokanɛ mǝ gbasi ɔwath yi ɔkara kɔŋ , mǝ kȧlanɛ ka ȧŋthɔf ŋa Isrɛl , kotȧy-e aŋfǝm aŋa thɛns tǝ kǝdif ɔwath-e aŋ po fi thɔŋ .
40002021	Kɔ yokanɛ ɔ gbasi ɔwath yi ɔkara kɔŋ-e , kɔ der ka ȧŋthɔf ŋa Isrɛl .
40002022	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ tǝl kǝpa Arkiliyɔsȧŋ ɔ sara ka aŋni ŋa ɔkas kɔŋ Herod-e , ɔ nesa tǝ kǝkɔ ri . Ɔwa ma Kuru ɔ maŋ kɔ rǝ mǝrey-e , ɔ kɔnɛ ka mȧgbȧp ma ro Kalili .
40002023	kɔ der , ɔ yirȧ ka kȧpet ȧke ma tela Nasarɛth ; kȧmȧ ȧrim ra ɔnȧbi rǝ lasǝr ara pa , A ba kǝbont kɔ uNasarɛth .
40003001	Ka mȧrey mati Yɔnȧŋ ɔBaftays ɔ wur gbafǝth , kɔ tamǝs ka aŋwula ŋa ro Yudia , ɔ pa ,
40003002	Thupi nu , kotȧy-e rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ po fat .
40003003	kotȧy-e ta ɔwe ɔnȧbi Aysayaŋ ɔ fɔf ma ɔ pa , Ȧrim ra ukin ɔwe gbelegbele ro wula , ɔ pa , Bɛnɛnɛ nu aroŋ da ɔMarki , Lompǝs nu asoŋ tɔŋ .
40003004	Yɔnȧŋ ɔ wɔŋ ruma ra aŋfon ŋa ȧyɔkmɛ , ɔwa ɔ senɛ ȧthɛbɛŋ ŋa areka . Ɛdi yɔŋ ɛ yi ɛlama yi rǝmai .
40003005	Ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati afǝm agbȧthi aŋ kɔ ro ŋɔŋ kǝwur ro Yerusalɛm yi ro Yudia bɛ , yi ka aŋgbaŋ bɛ aŋa fatǝr ro Yɔrdan .
40003006	kɔ baftays ŋa ro Yɔrdan maŋ gbithanɛ ɛhakɛ yaŋ .
40003007	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ nənk aFaresi yi aSadusi agbȧthi aŋ der kȧmȧ ɔ baftays ŋa , ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Naŋ , na rȧkomra ra ɛgbɔrɔ , kanɛ maŋ nu tǝ kǝgbukɛ rabaŋ ara mǝ der-e ?
40003008	Tiyȧŋ kȧrȧ nu mǝkomi mǝbeki ta kǝthupi .
40003009	Ɔwa te nu nanɛ ka ɛmerȧ ɛ nu kǝpa , Sǝ ba Ebraham ta ɔkas kȧsu ; kotȧy-e i kanɛ nu Kuruȧŋ ɔ gbǝli yokas awuth ta Ebraham ka masar ame .
40003010	Ɔwa ka-ake a po thɔ bot kabap ka aŋthǝŋk ŋa ɛyint . Tiyȧŋ , ŋǝnt o ŋǝnt aŋa mǝ te wur mǝkomi mǝfinɔ-e , a tǝ tap ŋi , a tǝ fitha ŋi ro nȧnt .
40003011	Minɛŋ yathi , i baftays nu yi mȧnt ka kǝthupi , kɛrɛ ɔwe mǝ der kǝdarǝŋ kȧmi kɔnɔ thasi mi afɔsɔ . I bek hɛ tǝ kǝwop ɛkɔftha yɔŋ . Ɔ tǝ baftays nu yi ɔYina mǝsǝm yi nȧnt .
40003012	Aŋfuŋa ŋɔŋ aŋ yi ka kȧta kɔŋ , ɔ tǝ gbǝl aŋgbethe ŋɔŋ gbǝraŋ , ɔwa ɔ tǝ thoŋkla apǝla pɔŋ ro fuŋk , kɛrɛ ɛfuk-e , ɔ tǝ thɔi yi rǝ nȧnt nǝte dimsɛ .
40003013	Ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ wur ro Kalili , ɔ der ro Yɔrdan ka Yɔn , kȧmȧ ɔ baftays kɔ .
40003014	Kɛrɛ Yɔnȧŋ ɔ yema bɛnt kɔ , ɔ pa , Pǝ mar munɔ mǝ baftays mi , kɛrɛ mǝ der ro mi-i ?
40003015	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Ta pǝ yi yaŋ ka-ake , kotȧy-e ya pǝ mar sǝ lasǝr mȧlompi bɛ . Kɔ selɔ ɔ baftays kɔ .
40003016	Ma a po baftays Yisɔs-e , ɔlɛmp wati ɔ wur ro mȧnt ; ka ȧkȧriyana kǝ kanthɛ , kɔ nənk ɔYina ka Kuru ɔ thor mɔ kǝpǝrǝm ɔ thorǝr kɔ ,
40003017	ka rim rǝ wur ka Kuru , rǝ pa , Ɔwe-e , kɔnɔ yi ɔWan kȧmi ubɔthǝr , ka ɔwe i ba mǝbɔnɛ .
40004001	Ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati ɔYina ɔ kera Yisɔsȧŋ ro wula kȧmȧ Sethani ɔ gbɔns kɔ .
40004002	Ma ɔ po wop asum mǝrei tǝgba tǝrǝŋ pali gbɛsȧŋ , dor rǝ wop kɔ .
40004003	Ka ɔgbɔns ɔ bek-e , ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Bepi munɔ yi ɔWan ka Kuru-e , yamari kȧmȧ masar ame mǝ sǝkɛ tǝbo .
40004004	Kɛrɛ Yisɔs ɔ pa , A po gbal kǝpa , Wuni ɔ ŋesǝm hɛ rǝ kǝbo gbo son , kɛrɛ rǝ rim o rim ara wur ka kasǝŋ ka Kuru .
40004005	Ka Sethaniȧŋ ɔ kera kɔ ka kȧpet kǝsǝm , kɔ tǝmǝr kɔ rokɔm ka ȧŋseth ŋa Kuru , ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ ,
40004006	Bepi mǝ yi ɔWan ka Kuru-e , tǝlpɛ roratha , kotȧy-e a po gbal kǝpa , Ɔ tǝ yamari aŋmȧleka ŋɔŋ ta ȧtȧ mu , Ɔwa aŋ tǝ kɛkǝr mu ka mȧta maŋ Ta thani mǝ gbuŋanɛ akatǝk ka mu rǝ ȧsar .
40004007	Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , A po sɔ gbal kǝpa , Te mɛmǝr ɔMarki ɔKuru ka mu .
40004008	Ka Sethaniȧŋ ɔ kera kɔ sɔ ka kǝteŋ kǝbɔli rǝkɔm , kɔ tɔri kɔ tabȧy bɛ ta ȧdȧru , yi ɛyiki yati .
40004009	kɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , I ti sɔŋ mu mayɛt ame bɛ-e bepi mǝ gbǝpsa , ɔwa mǝ bȧtho mi .
40004010	Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Sethani , sək mi rȧŋ ! kotȧy-e a po gbal kǝpa , Mǝ yi tǝ kǝbatho ɔMarki ɔKuru ka mu , ɔwa kɔnɔ gbo son mǝ mǝ yɔna .
40004011	Ka Sethaniȧŋ ɔ ter kɔ , ka aŋmȧleka aŋ der aŋ yɔna kɔ .
40004012	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tǝl kǝpa a bot Yɔnȧŋ ka ȧŋseth ŋa tǝrǝŋka-e , ɔ kɔnɛ ro Kalili .
40004013	kɔ wur ro Nasarɛth , ɔ der yirȧ ro Kepaniyɔm ȧke yi ro baŋ rayɛr , ka mȧnǝnkǝra ma ro Sɛbulɔn yi Nafthalim .
40004014	Kama tǝ lasǝr ȧte Isaya ɔnȧbi ɔ pa , kǝpa ,
40004015	Aŋthɔf ŋa ro Sɛbulɔn , yi ȧŋthɔf ŋa ro Nafthalim , Kǝbalǝr ro baŋ Yɔrdan mɔri , Ka Kalili ka tȧbona tǝlɔm ,
40004016	Aŋfǝm aŋa yirȧ ka ȧŋsum Aŋ nənk kǝwalɛ kǝbana ; Ɔwa kǝwalɛ kǝ put ro ŋaŋ Aŋa yirȧ ka ɔdɛr yi ka ȧŋmumpǝl ŋa rǝfi .
40004017	Kǝtəp ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tǝp kǝtam , ɔ pa , Thupi nu kotȧy-e rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ po fat .
40004018	Ɔwa ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ kɔth kɔth rayɛr ka kȧbȧŋ ka ro Kalili-e ɔ nənk awɔnt aruni ŋarǝŋ , Symɔnȧŋ ɔwe a bont Pita , yi Andrɔŋ ɔwɔnt kɔŋ , aŋ bɔ fitha kǝpɛl ro baŋ , kotȧy-e aŋ yi alǝm .
40004019	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , De nu tȧŋ mi , i ti yɔ nu nǝ lǝm afǝm .
40004020	Ɔlɛmp wati aŋ tey tapɛl ta naŋ , kaŋ tȧŋ kɔ .
40004021	Ma ɔ wur ri-e , ɔ nənk awɔnt aruni ŋarǝŋ alɔm , Yemǝsȧŋ ɔwan ka Sɛbidi , yi ɔwɔnt kɔŋ Yɔnȧŋ , aŋ yi ro bil dɛ yi Sɛbidi ɔkas ka ŋaŋ , aŋ bɔ gbɛŋgbǝlɛ tapɛl taŋ . Kɔ tela ŋa .
40004022	Ɔlɛmp wati aŋ tey ȧŋbil yi ɔkas ka ŋaŋ , kaŋ tȧŋ kɔ .
40004023	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ kɔth ro Kalili bɛ , ɔ thǝksa ka ɛseth ɛgbanɛ , ɔ tamǝs ȧkɛra kǝfinɔ ka rȧbȧy , ɔ yeŋkǝs rǝtu o rǝtu kətɔŋ ka aŋfəm .
40004024	Ka ȧŋes ŋɔŋ aŋ gbanthɛnɛ ro Siria bɛ ; kaŋ kȧrȧ ro ŋɔŋ aŋboma bɛ aŋa ba tǝtu yi ɛsɔmpanɛ ɛbaŋ ɛgbanthɛ tǝtǝp , ŋaŋ aŋa ba akǝrǝfi-o , tatuk-o , mȧthanthaŋ-o , ɔwa ɔ yeŋkǝs ŋa bɛ .
40004025	Ka suniya tǝbana tǝ tȧŋ kɔ kǝyɛfȧ ro Kalili , ro Dikapɔlis , ro Yerusalɛm , ro Yudia dɛ yi ro Yɔrdan mɔri .
40005001	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ nənk ȧsuniya-e , ɔ gbep ka kǝteŋ rokɔm . Ma ɔ po yira-e , aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ fatǝr kɔ .
40005002	kɔ tǝp kǝthǝksa ŋa , ɔ pa ,
40005003	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa yi amɔnɛ rǝ ȧmerȧ , kotȧy-e ŋa ba rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40005004	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa saŋ amɔl , kotȧy-e a ba kǝthɔnthɔ ŋa .
40005005	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa ba ɛmerȧ ɛthoranɛ , kotȧy-e aŋ tǝ ba ȧŋthɔf mɔ kɛŋ .
40005006	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa ba afela ta mȧlompi mɔ dor , kotȧy-e aŋ ba kǝnȧmrȧ .
40005007	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa ba ȧney , kotȧy-e a tǝ ba ŋa ȧney .
40005008	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa ba ɛmerȧ ɛfera , kotȧy-e aŋ ba kǝnǝŋk Kuru .
40005009	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa yi awom , kotȧy-e a tǝ bont ŋa aŋwuth ŋa Kuru .
40005010	Aruba ŋaŋ aŋa a po sɔmpa salata mȧlompi , kotȧy-e ŋa ba rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40005011	Nǝ ba aruba bepi a sambos nu , ɔwa a sɔmpa nu , thalɔm a fɔf nu ɔlǝs rǝ rǝyem salata mi .
40005012	Sel nu mǝbɔnɛ , ta pǝ bɔnɛ nu ɔthasǝr , kotȧy-e ȧŋram a nu aŋ yi ȧbana ro riyana ; ȧtesoma-e ya a sɔmpa aŋnabi aŋa yi thǝpaŋ .
40005013	Naŋ nǝ yi amɛr ma ȧdȧru , kɛrɛ bepi amɛr mǝ dim mabɔthi mati-e , ko rǝka rǝ mǝ bɔthǝs ma sɔ-e ? Mǝ thesa hɛ sɔ ta rǝka o rǝka thambe a fitha ma , ɔwa afǝm aŋ nas ma .
40005014	Naŋ nǝ yi ȧŋmothȧ ŋa ȧdȧru . Kȧpet ȧke yi ka kǝteŋ rokɔm-e kǝ gbǝli hɛ maŋknɛ .
40005015	Ɔwa afǝm aŋ moth hɛ kǝmulɛ tǝ kǝbot ki rǝ ȧthunthȧ roratha-e , thambe aŋ bot ki rǝ ɔtǝmǝr , kȧmȧ kǝ mothǝr ŋa bɛ ro seth .
40005016	Yɔ nu kȧmȧ ȧŋmothȧ a nu aŋ gbɛntha rodi ka aŋfǝm , kȧmȧ aŋ nənk mȧyɔs ma nu mǝfinɔ , ɔwa aŋ yikis ɔKas ka nu ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40005017	Te nu nanɛ kǝpa i der tǝ kǝlǝsǝr aŋthɔ , thalɔm tapa ta aŋnabi . I de hɛ tǝ kǝlǝsǝr , kɛrɛ tǝ kǝlasǝr .
40005018	Tɛntɛnɛ i pa ro rɔnu , Haŋ ȧkȧriyana yi ȧdȧru ɛ thas-e , hali tȧy tǝlɔl thalɔm agbal ŋin ŋa aŋthɔ aŋ gbǝli hɛ dinɛ haŋ a po lasǝr ŋi bɛ .
40005019	Tiyȧŋ wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ sim ȧgbȧp alɔl ŋin ŋa ɛthɔ ɛye , ama ɔ thǝksa afǝm yaŋ-e , a tǝ bont kɔ ulɔl ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana ; kɛrɛ ɔwe mǝ wop ama ɔ thǝksa yi-e , a tǝ bont kɔ ubana ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40005020	Tiyȧŋ i pa ro rɔnu , Thambe mȧlompi ma nu mǝ thas mȧlompi ma aŋkarmɔkɔ yi aŋFarisi-e , rǝ roŋ o roŋ nǝ gbǝli hɛ wɔŋ ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40005021	Nǝ po tǝl kǝpa a pa ka aŋbȧki thǝpaŋ , Te dif wuni . Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ dif wuni kǝsias-e , ɔ beki kȧmȧ ɔ sɔthɔ ȧthȧlǝr ka aŋthonkas .
40005022	Kɛrɛ minɛŋ i pa ro rɔnu , Wuni o wuni ɔwe ba mǝbaŋ ta ɔwɔnt kɔŋ-e , ɔ tǝ fumpɔ kasi ro bare ; ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ farki ɔwɔnt kɔŋ-e , ɔ tǝ fumpɔ kasi ka aŋSanhedrin ; kɛrɛ wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ pa , Mun pǝŋk , ɔ tǝ fumpɔ kasi ro yahanama .
40005023	Tiyȧŋ bepi mǝ kȧrȧ ȧŋboya a mu ka ȧŋbɛsɛ-e , ɔwa mǝ kala ȧmerȧ kǝpa ɔwɔnt mu ɔ ba mǝbaŋ ta ȧtȧ mu-e ;
40005024	tey ri ȧŋboya a mu , kɔnɛ mǝ mɔtha kȧl manɛ yi ɔwɔnt mu , kǝdarǝŋ kati mǝ der , mǝ sɔŋ ȧŋboya a mu .
40005025	Manɛ yi ɔtheranɛ ka mu ka ȧŋlɔkɔ na mǝ taŋanɛ ro roŋ yi kɔn ; ta thani ɔtheranɛ ka mu ɔ lȧnki mu ka ɔthoŋkas , ɔwa ɔthoŋkas ɔ lȧnki mu ka ȧŋbɔy , ɔwa a tand mu ka ȧŋseth ŋa tǝrǝŋka .
40005026	Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ mu , mǝ ba hɛ kǝwur ri rǝ roŋ o roŋ haŋ mǝ poŋ ram aŋwankɔpɔ alǝpsɔ .
40005027	Nǝ po tǝl kǝpa a pa , Te yɔ kǝrǝp .
40005028	Kɛrɛ minɛȧŋ i pa ro rɔnu , Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ kǝli wuni bom tǝ kǝfela kɔ-e , ɔ po yɔ kǝrǝp ka ȧŋmerȧ ŋɔŋ .
40005029	Bepi rafɔr ra mu rǝdiɔ rǝ yɔ mu mǝ pǝnthbǝla-e , kothi ri , fitha ri , kotȧy-e pǝ tǝ fisa mu bepi abɛm ŋin ŋa aŋdɛr a mu aŋ lǝsȧ-e , pǝthasi kǝfitha aŋdɛr a mu alolok ro yahanama .
40005030	Ɔwa bepi kȧta ka mu kǝdiyɔ kǝ yɔ mu mǝ pǝnthbǝla-e , gbǝk ki , fitha ki , kotȧy-e pǝ tǝ fisa mu bepi abɛm ŋin ŋa aŋdɛr a mu aŋ lǝsǝ pǝthasi kǝfitha aŋdɛr a mu alolok ro yahanama .
40005031	A po pa sɔ , Bepi wuni o wuni ɔ ter ɔrani kɔŋ-e , ta ɔ sɔŋ kɔ areka ŋa kasakanɛ ;
40005032	kɛrɛ minɛȧŋ i pa ro rɔnu , Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ ter ɔrani kɔŋ pǝ yi hɛ tȧ kǝrǝp-e , ɔ yɔ ɔbɛra ɔ sǝkɛ urǝpi , ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ nȧntȧ kɔ ɔwe a po ter-e , ɔ yɔ kǝrǝp .
40005033	Nǝ po tǝl kǝpa a pa ka aŋbȧki thǝpaŋ , Te gbiŋ kǝgbiŋ ka rǝyem , kɛrɛ lasǝr ɛgbiŋ ɛ nu ka ɔMarki .
40005034	Kɛrɛ minɛȧŋ i pa ro rɔnu , Te gbiŋ hali , pǝ yi hɛ ka ȧkȧriyana , kotȧy-e kǝ yi kawaŋ ka rȧbȧy ra Kuru Mǝsaba ,
40005035	pǝ yi hɛ ka ȧdȧru , kotȧy-e kǝ yi kȧpet ka ɔBȧy ubana .
40005036	Te gbiŋ ka rȧbomp ra mu , pǝkasifɛ mǝ gbǝli hɛ sǝki rafon ra mu rin rǝfera thalɔm rǝbi .
40005037	Kɛrɛ ta mapa ma mu mǝ yi Yao , Yao , thalɔm Yi thahɔ , Yi thahɔ ; kotȧy-e tȧy o tȧy ȧte thas ȧte tǝ wur ka ɔlǝs .
40005038	Nǝ po tǝl kǝpa a pa , Rǝfɔr ta rǝfɔr , rǝsek ta rǝsek ;
40005039	kɛrɛ minɛȧŋ i pa ro rɔnu , Te kasi mǝlǝs . Bepi wuni o wuni ɔ gbantha mu ka aŋkos ȧdiyɔ-e , lȧfthɛ kɔ aŋlɔm sɔ .
40005040	Ɔwa bepi wuni o wuni ɔ kera mu ro bare-e , ɔwa ɔ nɔy mu aruma ra mu-e , yɔ kȧmȧ ɔ ba sɔ kafɔl ka mu .
40005041	Bepi wuni o wuni ɔ kithinɛ mu tǝ kǝpȧyȧ kɔ ȧmayl ŋin-e , pȧyȧ kɔ yɛrǝŋ .
40005042	Sɔŋ ka ɔwe mǝ tholir mu , te pɛnsa ɔwuni ɔwe yema bɔr mu .
40005043	Nǝ po tǝl kǝpa a pa , Bɔthǝr ɔfatanɛ ka mu , ɔwa gbɛŋa ɔtheranɛ ka mu .
40005044	Kɛrɛ minɛȧŋ i pa ro nu , Bɔthǝr aŋtheranɛ a nu , ɔwa ramnɛ nu ta ȧtȧ ŋaŋ aŋa sɔmpa nu ,
40005045	kȧmȧ nǝ yi aŋwuth ŋa ɔKas ka nu ɔwe yi ro riyana . Kotȧy-e ɔ yɔ aret rɔŋ rǝ putǝr ka aŋlǝs yi ka aŋfinɔ , ɔ somra akɔm ka aŋlompi yi ka aŋkǝnȧ .
40005046	Ȧtesoma-e bepi nǝ bɔthǝr gbo aŋa bɔthǝr nu-e , ko ȧrȧm naŋ mǝ nǝ sɔthɔ-e ? Yaŋ tha aŋthoŋkla ɛfȧk aŋ yɔ sɔ-e ?
40005047	Bepi nǝ kori aŋwɔnt nu gbo-e , ko tȧy tǝfinɔ tȧŋ nǝ yɔ pǝthas alɔm-e ? Yaŋ tha tȧbona tǝlɔm mǝ aŋ yɔ sɔ-e ?
40005048	Tiyȧŋ yi nu agbenthis mɔ mǝ ɔKas ka nu ɔwe yi ro riyana ɔ yi ugbenthis .
40006001	Botnɛ nu kȧmȧ nǝ te yɔ mȧlompi ma nu rodi ka aŋfǝm kȧmȧ aŋ nənk nu . Bepi pǝ yi yaŋ-e , nǝ sɔthɔ hɛ ȧrȧm kǝwur ka ɔKas ka nu ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40006002	Tiyȧŋ ma mǝ nǝ sɔŋ ɛboya-e , te nu fɛŋ kǝthɛma rodi ka nu mɔ mǝ ȧŋmunafȧki mǝ aŋ yɔ ka ɛseth ɛgbanɛ yi ka asoŋ-e , kȧmȧ aŋ sɔthɔ ayiki ka aŋfǝm . Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , aŋ po sɔthɔ ȧŋrȧm ŋaŋ .
40006003	Kɛrɛ ma mǝ mǝ sɔŋ ɛboya-e , te selɔ kȧta ka mu kǝmɛrɔ kǝ tȧrȧ ȧte kȧta ka mu kǝdiyɔ kǝ yɔ ;
40006004	kȧmȧ ɛboya ɛ nu ɛ yi rǝ agbundu , ɔwa ɔKas ka nu ɔwe nənk rǝ agbundu ɔ tǝ ram nu gbafǝth .
40006005	Ɔwa ma nǝ ramnɛ-e , te nu yi mɔ ȧŋmunafȧki , kotȧy-e aŋ bɔther kǝtǝma ka ɛseth ɛgbanɛ yi ka asoŋ tǝsakanɛ kȧmȧ aŋfǝm aŋ nənk ŋa . Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , aŋ po sɔthɔ ȧŋrȧm ŋaŋ .
40006006	Kɛrɛ munɔŋ , bepi mǝ ramnɛ-e , wɔŋ ka ȧŋkonko a mu , ɔwa ma mǝ po kantha kadare ka mu-e , ramnɛ ka ɔKas ka mu ɔwe yi rǝ ɔmaŋknɛ , ɔwa ɔKas ka mu ɔwe nənk rǝ ɔmaŋknɛ ɔ tǝ ram mu gbafǝth .
40006007	Kɛrɛ ma nǝ ramnɛ-e , te nu fɔf sim tǝgbathi tǝyai , mɔ mǝ tȧbona tǝlɔm mǝ tǝ yɔ ; kotȧy-e aŋ nanɛ kǝpa a tǝ tǝla ŋa ta tafɔf taŋ tǝgbathi .
40006008	Tiyȧŋ te nu yi mɔ ŋaŋ , ȧtesoma-e ɔKas ka nu ɔ tȧrȧ ɛyɛt ɛyɛ nǝ yema yeŋka nǝ yif kɔ .
40006009	Tiyȧŋ ramnɛ nu yaŋ ; ƆKas kȧsu ɔwe yi ro riyana , kanka ȧŋes a mu aŋ yi ȧsǝm .
40006010	Kaŋkɔ rȧbȧy ra mu rǝ bek . Kaŋkɔ mȧselɔ ma mu mǝ yɔnɛ nɔru mɔ mǝ mǝ yɔnɛ ro riyana .
40006011	Yer su thonɔŋ ɛyɛt ɛdi ɛbeki su .
40006012	Tera su mȧtȧy ma su mǝlǝs , mɔ saŋ mǝ sǝ tera ŋaŋ aŋa yɔ su ɔlǝs .
40006013	Te su wɔŋȧ rǝ tȧy tǝgbɔns kɛrɛ wurɔ su ka mətȧy mǝlǝs ; ȧtesoma-e munɔ ba rȧbȧy yi aŋfɔsɔ yi aŋyiki thȧnkȧŋ thǝbana , Amina .
40006014	kotȧy-e , bepi nǝ tera afǝm mȧtȧy maŋ mǝlǝs-e , ɔKas ka nu ro riyana ɔ tǝ tera nu sɔ ,
40006015	kɛrɛ bepi nǝ tera hɛ afǝm mȧtȧy maŋ mǝlǝs-e , ɔKas ka nu ɔ ba hɛ kǝtera nu mȧtȧy ma nu mǝlǝs .
40006016	Ɔwa ma pǝ thas ri-e , bepi nǝ wop asum-e , te nu suma mɔ aŋyɔr ; kotȧy-e aŋ lǝsǝr aser taŋ kȧmȧ aŋfǝm aŋ nənk kǝpa aŋ wop asum . Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu kǝpa aŋ po sɔthɔ ȧŋrȧm ŋaŋ .
40006017	Kɛrɛ munɔŋ , bepi mǝ wop asum , sop rȧbomp ra mu yi mȧro , ɔwa yak ȧder a mu ,
40006018	kȧmȧ afǝm aŋ te nənk kǝpa mǝ wop asum-e , kɛrɛ ɔKas ka mu ɔwe yi rǝ ɔmaŋknɛ . Ɔwa ɔKas ka mu ɔwe nənk rǝ agbundu ɔ tǝ ram mu .
40006019	Te nu thoŋklanɛ tɛŋ ka ȧdȧru ro amɔrka yi magbak mȧ mǝ sɔm ti , dɛ yi akey mǝ aŋ bɛs tǝ kǝkeya .
40006020	Thoŋklanɛ nu gbo tɛŋ ro riyana , ro amɔrka yi mǝgbak mǝ gbǝli hɛ sɔm ti , ɔwa ro akey aŋ te bɛs , aŋ keya .
40006021	Ȧtesoma-e ro atɛŋ ta nu tǝ yi-e , rǝ ɛmerȧ ɛ nu ɛ tǝ yi sɔ .
40006022	ȧŋmothȧ ŋa aŋdɛr aŋ yi rafɔr . Tiyȧŋ bepi rafɔr ra mu rǝ yi rǝtempi-e , rǝ tǝ mothǝr aŋdɛr a mu bɛ .
40006023	Kɛrɛ bepi rafɔr ra mu rǝ yi rǝlǝs-e , aŋdɛr a mu bɛ aŋ tǝ la asum . Tiyȧŋ bepi ȧŋmothȧ aŋa yi mu aŋ yi asum-e , ȧŋsum ŋati a bana !
40006024	Wuni o wuni ɔ gbǝli hɛ bȧtho amarki ŋarǝŋ , kotȧy-e ɔ tǝ gbɛŋa ɔkin ɔwa ɔ tǝ bɔthǝr ɔlɔm ; thalɔm ɔ tǝ gbapsa ɔkin , ɔwa ɔ tǝ sai ɔlɔm . Nǝ gbǝli hɛ bȧtho Kuru dɛ yi mǝbɔŋɔ .
40006025	Tiyȧŋ i kanɛ nu , te nu ba asoli ta ɛŋesǝm ɛ nu , ta ara mǝ nǝ di-e , thalɔm ta ara mǝ nǝ mun-e , ta a pa ras ta aŋdɛr a nu ta ara mǝ nǝ wɔŋ . Aŋesǝm aŋ thas hɛ yɛt ɛdi-i , ɔwa aŋdɛr aŋ thas hɛ ɛloprȧ-i ?
40006026	Kǝli ɛbȧmp rokɔm-a , aŋ sak hɛ , aŋ rɔk hɛ , aŋ thonkla hɛ rǝ tǝfunk : kɛrɛ ɔKas ka nu ro riyana ɔ wɔnthǝr ŋa . Naŋ-e , nǝ thas hɛ ŋa mȧrǝŋ mȧrǝŋ-i ?
40006027	Wuni reke kǝtɔŋ kȧnu mǝ gbǝli bȧr alonk ŋin ka kasaŋa kɔŋ , hali ɔ ba ti afela-e ?
40006028	Ɔwa kɔyɛŋ nǝ ba asoli ta yɛt ɛloprȧ-e ? Tȧmtȧmnɛ tȧyaba ta ro lal ma mǝ tǝ lɔkɔ ; tǝ yɔ hɛ mǝpanth , tǝ sǝrǝm hɛ ,
40006029	kɛrɛ i kanɛ nu-e , hali Sɔlɔmɔn ka aŋyiki ŋɔŋ bɛ ɔ lopra hɛ mɔ malɛŋi mati ame .
40006030	Ɔwa bepi Kuruȧŋ ɔ lonsǝr akereŋ ka ro lal yaŋ-e , ȧke yi thonɔŋ , ɔwa ninaŋ a fitha ki rǝ nȧnt nǝbana ; thamsinɛ naŋ-e , nia afǝm ŋa kǝlanɛ kǝthan .
40006031	Tiyȧŋ te nu soli kǝpa , Ko mǝ sǝ di-e , thalɔm ko mǝ sǝ mun-e , ta a pa ras ko mǝ sǝ wɔŋ-e ?
40006032	kotȧy-e ɛyɛt ɛye bɛ-e , yɛ tȧbona tǝlɔm mǝ tǝ thɛns , kɛrɛ ɔKas ka nu ro riyana ɔ tȧrȧ kǝpa nǝ yema ɛyɛt ɛye bɛ .
40006033	Kɛrɛ mɔtha nu thɛns rȧbȧy ra Kuru , dɛ yi mȧlompi mɔŋ , ɔwa ɔ tǝ bȧrȧ nu ɛyɛt ɛye bɛ .
40006034	Tiyȧŋ te nu ba asoli ta ninaŋ , ȧtesoma-e rasɔk ra ninaŋ rǝ tǝ ba aŋsoli ŋati . Mȧlǝs ma ȧŋrey mǝ beki ta ȧŋrey ŋati .
40007001	Te nu thonkas wuni , kȧmȧ a te thonkas nu .
40007002	kotȧy-e kathoŋkas ȧke mǝ nǝ thoŋkas-e kǝ mǝ a thonkas nu ; ɔwa aŋthuntha aŋa mǝ nǝ thunth-e , ŋǝ mǝ a kȧl thuntha nu .
40007003	Ko tȧy tȧŋ mǝ nənk ȧŋpol aŋa yi ka rafɔr ra ɔwɔnt mu kɛrɛ mǝ te nənk kagboŋ ȧke yi ka rafɔr ra mu gbeŋ-e ?
40007004	Thalɔm to mǝ gbǝli pa ka ɔwɔnt mu , Yɔ kȧmȧ i wurɔ ȧŋpol ka rafɔr ra mu , ma mǝ ba kagboŋ ka rafɔr ra mu-e ?
40007005	Mun wuni yɔr , mɔtha wurɔ kagboŋ ka rafɔr ra mu , ɔwa kǝdarǝŋ kati mǝ tǝ gbǝli nənk gbǝraŋ tǝ kǝwura ȧŋpol ka rafɔr ra ɔwɔnt mu .
40007006	Te nu sɔŋ rǝka rǝsǝm ka ɛtǝn , ɔwa te fitha mȧthǝni ma nu ka tǝsɔp , ta thani aŋ nas ma ka ȧtȧtək taŋ , ɔwa aŋ fǝlɛ aŋ gbarigbari nu .
40007007	Yif nu , a tǝ sɔŋ nu . Thɛns nu , ɔwa nǝ tǝ fir . Gbȧtgbȧt nu ka kȧdare , a tǝ kanthɛ nu ;
40007008	kotȧy-e wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ yif-e , ɔ tǝ sɔthɔ , ɔwe mǝ thɛns-e , ɔ tǝ fir , ɔwa ɔwe mǝ gbatgbat-e , a tǝ kanthɛ kɔ .
40007009	Wuni reke kǝtɔŋ ka nu-e , bepi ɔwan kɔŋ ɔ tholir kɔ kǝbo-e , mǝ ɔ sɔŋ kɔ asar-e ?
40007010	Thalɔm bepi ɔ tholir kɔ kǝlop-e , mǝ ɔ sɔŋ kɔ abok-e ?
40007011	Bepi naŋ ma nǝ yi alǝs-e , nǝ tȧrȧ kǝsɔŋ ɛboya ɛfinɔ ka aŋwuth a nu-e , pǝ tha gbethi ɔKas ka nu ɔwe yi ro riyana mǝ ɔ sɔŋ hɛ ɛyɛt ɛfinɔ ka ŋaŋ aŋa mǝ tholir kɔ-i ?
40007012	Tiyȧŋ tȧy o tȧy ȧte nǝ yema kȧmȧ afǝm aŋ yɔ nu-e , ya nǝ yi tǝ kǝyɔ sɔ ro ŋaŋ ; kotȧy-e ȧte tǝ yi aŋthɔ yi ɛmaŋ ya aŋnabi .
40007013	Wɔŋ nu ka kadare kǝthiŋkanɛ , kotȧy-e kadare kǝ yi kǝbana ɔwa aroŋ rǝ yi rǝbana ara lomanɛ ka kadinɛ , ɔwa ŋa agbȧthi aŋa wɔŋ ri .
40007014	Pǝkasifɛ kadare kǝ thiŋkanɛ ɔwa aroŋ rǝ lɔl ara lomanɛ ka aŋesǝm , ɔwa ŋa athȧn aŋa fir ri .
40007015	Botnɛ nu rǝ ȧmerȧ ta aŋnabi ayem aŋa mǝ der ro nu rǝ ɛlopra ya tǝlɔmɛ , kɛrɛ rokor aŋ yi tǝthɔlu alukǝs .
40007016	Nǝ tǝ tȧrȧ ŋa ka mȧkomi maŋ . Afǝm aŋ gbǝli pim mǝtiti rǝ tǝbȧnk-i , thalɔm mǝgbɔnɔ rǝ tǝsenduku-i ?
40007017	Ya pǝ yi sɔ-e , ŋǝnt o ŋǝnt afinɔ aŋ kom mǝkomi mǝfinɔ , kɛrɛ ŋǝnt alǝs aŋ kom mǝkomi mǝlǝs .
40007018	Ŋǝnt afinɔ aŋ gbǝli hɛ kom mǝkomi mǝlǝs , ya pǝ yi sɔ , ŋǝnt alǝs aŋ gbǝli hɛ kom mǝkomi mǝfinɔ .
40007019	Ŋǝnt o ŋǝnt aŋa te kom mǝkomi mǝfinɔ-e , a tǝ tap ŋi , ɔwa a tǝ fitha ŋi ro nȧnt .
40007020	Tiyȧŋ nǝ tǝ tȧrȧ ŋa ka mȧkomi maŋ .
40007021	Pǝ yi hɛ wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ pa ro mi , Pa , Pa , kɔnɔ mǝ wɔŋ ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana , kɛrɛ ŋaŋ gbo son aŋa mǝ yɔ mȧselɔ ma ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40007022	Agbȧthi aŋ tǝ pa ro rɔmi ka ȧŋrey ŋati , Pa , Pa , saŋ-e , sǝ la hɛ nȧbi ka ȧŋes a mu-i ? Sǝ la hɛ wurɔ akǝrǝfi-i , sǝ la hɛ yɔ mǝyɔs mǝkabanɛ mǝgbathi ka ȧŋes a mu-i ?
40007023	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati i ti kanɛ ŋa gbafǝth kǝpa , Thȧnkȧŋ i tɛ hɛ nu . Wur nu ro rɔmi , naŋ aŋa yɔ mǝyɔs mǝlǝs .
40007024	Tiyȧŋ wuni o wuni ɔwe tǝl ȧsim ta mi-e , ɔwa ɔ wop ti-e , ɔ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ wuni tempi ɔwe tǝmǝr ȧŋseth ŋɔŋ ka aŋgbalaŋ rokɔm .
40007025	Ka akɔm kǝ thuf , ɔwa ȧmȧnt mǝfɔl mǝ der , ka aŋfef aŋ sɔŋ aŋ sapǝth ȧŋseth ŋati ; kɛrɛ aŋ fumpɔ hɛ , ȧtesoma-e a tǝmǝr ŋi ka aŋgbalaŋ rokɔm .
40007026	Kɛrɛ wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ tǝl ȧsim ta mi ȧte , ɔwa ɔ wop hɛ ti-e , ɔ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ wuni pǝŋk ɔwe tǝmǝr ȧŋseth ŋɔŋ ka kȧsǝnt .
40007027	Ka akɔm kǝ thuf , ɔwa ȧmȧnt mǝfɔl mǝ der , ka aŋfef aŋ sɔŋ , aŋ sȧpǝth ȧŋseth ŋati . Kaŋ fumpɔ , ɔwa kȧfumpɔ kati kǝ yi kǝbana .
40007028	Ka pǝ re yi ma Yisɔs ɔ gbanthi ȧsim ȧte , aŋfǝm aŋ kabanɛ ta kathǝksa kɔŋ ,
40007029	kotȧy-e ɔ thǝksa ŋa mɔ wuni ɔwe ba afɔsɔ , pǝ yi hɛ mɔ aŋkarmɔkɔ aŋ yɔ .
40008001	Ɔwa ma ɔ thor ka kateŋ-e , suniya tǝbana tǝ tan kɔ .
40008002	Ka wuni ka rǝlel ɔ der ro ŋɔŋ , ɔ sɔna kɔ tǝwu , kɔ pa , Pa , bepi mǝ selɔ-e , mǝ gbǝli fethǝr mi .
40008003	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ thanthi kȧta kɔŋ , ɔ gboŋ kɔ , kɔ pa , I selɔ . Yi mun gbǝraŋ . Ka ɔlɛmp wati ralel rǝ pond kɔ .
40008004	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro rɔŋɔŋ , Botnɛ kȧmȧ mǝ te kanɛ ti wuni o wuni , kɛrɛ kɔnɛ mǝ tɔrinɛ ka aŋfode , kȧmȧ mǝ wurɔ asathka ȧte Mosisȧŋ ɔ yamari tǝ kǝyi mǝseri ro ŋaŋ .
40008005	Ɔwa ma ɔ wɔŋ ro Kapǝrneɔm-e , ukaptin ɔ der ro ŋɔŋ , kɔ nɛmthɛnɛ kɔ , ɔ pa ,
40008006	Pa , ȧŋbɔy a mi ɔ fǝntha ro seth kȧmi , ɔ po gbɛthkɛ , ɔwa ɔ nakasi ɔthasǝr .
40008007	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , I ti der yeŋkǝs kɔ .
40008008	Ka ɔkaptin ɔ pa , Pa , i bek hɛ kǝpa munɔ mǝ wɔŋ ka ȧŋseth a mi . Pa gbo ȧrim , ɔwa ȧŋbɔy a mi ɔ tǝ yeŋk .
40008009	kotȧy-e minɛ sɔ i yi wuni ka afɔsɔ ratha , i ba aturgba roratha kȧmi . Ma i pa ka ɔkin ɔwe , Kɔnɛ , ɔwa ɔ tǝ kɔ . Ka ɔlɔm , Der , ɔwa ɔ tǝ der . Ka ȧŋbɔy a mi , Yɔ ȧte , ɔwa ɔ tǝ yɔ ti .
40008010	Ma Yisɔs ɔ tǝl ȧte , ɔ kabanɛ , kɔ pa ka ŋaŋ aŋa tȧŋ kɔ-e , Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i pa ro rɔnu , i tha bǝp hɛ kǝlanɛ kǝbana kǝwunɔŋ , hali kǝtɔŋ ka aŋIsrɛl bɛ .
40008011	Ɔwa i kanɛ nu , agbȧthi aŋ tǝ wur ro thɔrɔŋ yi ro pil , aŋ tǝ yirȧ yi Ebraham , yi Aysak dɛ yi Yekɔb ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana ,
40008012	kɛrɛ a tǝ fitha aŋwuth ŋa rȧbȧy ka ȧŋsum rokaŋ , ro kǝkulɔ yi kȧŋȧkŋȧk ɛsek kǝ yi .
40008013	Ka ȧŋbɔy ŋɔŋ ɔ yeŋk ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati gbeŋ .
40008014	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ wɔŋ ka ȧŋseth ŋa Pitar-e , ɔ nənk ɔniŋkara kɔŋ ɔ fǝntha , ɔ tu mǝdɛr mǝgbipanɛ .
40008015	kɔ gboŋ kȧta kɔŋ , ka madɛr mǝgbipanɛ mǝ ter kɔ , kɔ yokanɛ , ɔ yɔna kɔ .
40008016	Ma rȧfɔy rǝ bek-e , a kȧrȧ kɔ afǝm agbȧthi aŋa ba akǝrǝfi . Kɔ wurɔ aŋkǝrǝfi rǝ rim , ɔ kȧl yeŋkǝs aŋa yi aboma bɛ ;
40008017	kȧmȧ ȧte Isaya ɔnȧbi ɔ pa tǝ lasǝr , kǝpa , Kɔn kɔnɔnɛ ɔ gbasi mȧrȧnt ma su , ɔwa ɔ sara tatu ta su .
40008018	Ɔwa , ma Yisɔs ɔ nənk suniya tǝbana tǝ gbǝtɔsnɛ kɔ-e , ɔ yamari tǝ kǝfǝsi romɔri .
40008019	Ka ukarmɔkɔ ulɔm ɔ der , ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Karmɔkɔ i ti tȧŋ mu dɛr o dɛr ro maŋ kɔ .
40008020	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro rɔŋɔŋ hɔ , Ɛgbogboro aŋ ba tǝyaŋka-e , ɛbȧmp ya aŋfena aŋ ba ɛseth . Kɛrɛ ɔWan ka wuni ɔ ba hɛ dɛr ro mǝ ɔ bot rȧbomp rɔŋ .
40008021	Ka ulɔm ka aŋkarande ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Pa , ter mi kȧmȧ i mɔtha kɔ maŋk ɔkas kȧmi .
40008022	Kɛrɛ Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Tȧŋ mi , ɔwa tey aŋfi kȧmȧ aŋ kɔ maŋk aŋfi ŋaŋ .
40008023	Ɔwa ma ɔ po bȧkȧ rǝ abil-e , aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ tȧŋ kɔ .
40008024	Kɛrɛ ka ɔlɛmp wati kǝnkǝl kǝbana kǝ yokanɛ ro baŋ , haŋ ɛmuŋkǝl ɛ gbǝpǝr ȧŋbil : kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ bɔ dirȧ .
40008025	kaŋ kɔ thǝmi kɔ , aŋ pa , Pa , kisis su , sǝ dinɛ .
40008026	Kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , kɔyɛŋ mǝ nǝ nesa-e , naŋ aŋa ba kǝlanɛ kǝthan-e ? Kɔ yokanɛ , ɔ ŋal aŋfef yi kȧbȧŋ . Ka pǝ re yi ɔthɔfǝl bɛm .
40008027	Ka aŋfǝm aŋ kabanɛ , aŋ pa , Ko wuni wɔŋ ɔwe-e , ɔwe pǝ yi hali aŋfef yi kȧbȧŋ aŋ tǝla kɔ-e ?
40008028	Ma ɔ po fǝsi romɔri ka ȧŋthɔf ŋa aŋKadarin-e , afǝm ŋarǝŋ aŋa ba akǝrǝfi aŋ wur ka taboma , aŋ gbanɛ kɔ . Aŋ yi aninis ɔthasǝr , ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔ gbǝli hɛ thas ka aroŋ dati .
40008029	kaŋ sel ɛrɔŋ , aŋ pa , Ko tȧy tȧŋ saŋ sǝ ba yi munɔȧŋ-e , munɔ Yisɔs ɔWan ka Kuru-e ? Mǝ po der nɔ tǝ kǝsɔmpa su yeŋka ȧŋlɔkɔ aŋ bek-i ?
40008030	Ɔwa kuthi ka tǝsɔp agbȧthi kǝ yi ri , kǝ bɔ wɔnth dɛr ɔbɔlanɛ poŋ .
40008031	Ka aŋkǝrǝfi aŋ nɛmthɛnɛ kɔ aŋ pa , Bepi mǝ wurɔ su-e , ter su kȧmȧ sǝ kɔ wɔŋ ka akuthi ka tǝsɔp .
40008032	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Kɔnɛ . Kaŋ wur , kaŋ wɔŋ ka tǝsɔp . Ɔwa akuthi ka tǝsop kǝ gbuŋklɛ kǝder ka aŋtǝmp ŋa ro baŋ , kaŋ dinɛ ro mȧnt .
40008033	Ka ŋa aŋa bumǝr ŋa-e aŋ gbukɛ aŋ kɔ ro pet , aŋ tɔri koko bɛ , dɛ yi ȧte yɔnɛ ŋaŋ aŋa la ba aŋkǝrǝfi .
40008034	Ka aŋfǝm bɛ ro pet aŋ wur tǝ kǝgbans Yisɔsȧŋ . Maŋ nənk kɔ-e , aŋ nɛmthɛnɛ kɔ kȧmȧ ɔ wur ka ȧŋthɔf ŋaŋ .
40009001	kɔ bȧkȧ ka abil , ɔ fǝsi romɔri , kɔ der ka kȧpet kɔŋ .
40009002	Kaŋ kȧrȧ ulaŋgba ro ŋɔŋ ugbɛthkɛ ɔ fǝntha rǝ kǝfǝnt . Ma Yisɔs ɔ nənk kȧlanɛ ka ŋaŋ-e , ɔ pa ka ɔlaŋgba , Wan , bȧk kǝbuth . A po tera mu ɛhakɛ ɛ mu .
40009003	Ka aŋkarmɔkɔ alɔm aŋ pa ka ɛmerȧ yaŋ , Ɔlaŋgba ɔwe ɔ thunthǝra Kuru .
40009004	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tȧrȧ ɛnanɛ yaŋ-e , ɔ pa , To pǝ som mǝ nǝ nanɛ ɔlǝs ka ɛmerȧ ɛ nu-e ?
40009005	Rǝ reke tha yi rǝfɔi tai-e , tǝ kǝpa , A po tera mu ɛhakɛ ɛ mu , thalɔm tǝ kǝpa , Yokanɛ , mǝ kɔth-e ?
40009006	Kɛrɛ kȧmȧ nǝ tȧrȧ kǝpa ɔWan ka wuni ɔ ba afɔsɔ nɔru tǝ kǝtera wuni ɛhakɛ-e , ( kɔ pa ka ɔwe po gbɛthǝkɛ-e ) Yokanɛ , mǝ gbasi kafǝnt ka mu , mǝ kɔ ro seth ka mu .
40009007	kɔ yokanɛ , ɔ kɔnɛ ro seth kɔŋ .
40009008	Kɛrɛ ma ȧsuniya aŋ nənk ti-e , aŋ kabanɛ , kaŋ yikis Kuruȧŋ ɔwe po sɔŋ afɔsɔ awunɔŋ ka afǝm .
40009009	Ɔwa ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ wur ri-e , ɔ nənk wuni ɔwe a bont Mathiu , ɔ yirȧ ka ɔdɛr ro mǝ a gbasi ɛfȧk . Kɔ pa ro rɔŋɔŋ , Taŋ mi . Kɔ yokanɛ , ɔ tȧŋ kɔ .
40009010	Ka pǝ re yi ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ yirȧ ka kǝdi ro seth-e , afǝm aŋa gbasi ɛfȧk yi afǝm ŋa ɛhakɛ agbȧthi aŋ der aŋ yirȧ yi kɔn dɛ yi aŋkarande ŋɔŋ .
40009011	Ma aŋFarisi aŋ nənk ti-e , aŋ pa ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , To pǝ som ɔkarmɔkɔ ka nu mǝ ɔ di yi ŋaŋ aŋa gbasi ɛfȧk dɛ yi afǝm ŋa ɛhakɛ-e ?
40009012	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tǝl ti-e , ɔ pa , Ŋaŋ aŋa yi ayenki mǝdɛr aŋ yema hɛ udamǝr , kɛrɛ aŋtui ŋa yema udamǝr .
40009013	Kɛrɛ kɔnɛ nu kȧmȧ nǝ kɔ thǝkǝs ȧte , I yema ȧney , sathka thahɔ ; ȧtesoma-e i der hɛ tǝ kǝmuti aŋlompi-e , kɛrɛ i der tǝ kǝmuti aŋfǝm ŋa ɛhakɛ tǝ kǝthupi .
40009014	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati aŋkarande ŋa Yɔn aŋ der ro ŋɔŋ , aŋ pa , To som saŋ yi aŋFarisi sǝ wop asum katkat , kɛrɛ aŋkarande a mu aŋ wop hɛ asum-e ?
40009015	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Aŋyathki ŋa ɔnȧntȧ aŋ gbǝli saŋ amɔl ma ɔnȧntȧ ɔ yi ras yi ŋaŋ-i ? Kɛrɛ mȧrey mǝ tǝ der ma mǝ a nɔy ŋa ɔnȧntȧ , ɔwa ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati aŋ tǝ wop asum .
40009016	Wuni ɔ gbap hɛ arombo ŋa kotha kǝfu rǝ ruma rǝkur , kotȧy-e ȧŋrombo ŋati aŋ tǝ pim aruma , ɔwa ɔpima ɔ tǝ bȧr gbo lǝsǝ .
40009017	Ɔwa a bot hɛ mǝwain mǝfɛth rǝ tǝbos tǝkur ; bepi pǝ yi ti-e , tabos tǝ tǝ puta , ɔwa mawain mǝ tǝ loŋa , dɛ yi tabos tǝ tǝ lǝsǝ ; kɛrɛ a bot mǝwain mǝfɛth rǝ tǝbos tǝfu , ɔwa yi yɛrǝŋ ɛ tǝ won .
40009018	Ma ɔ kanɛ ŋa mȧtȧy ame-e , ugbǝka ulɔm ɔ der , ɔ sɔna kɔ tǝwu , ɔ pa , Ɔwan kȧmi ubɛra ɔ fi ka-ake , kɛrɛ der reŋ kɔ kȧta kȧmu kȧmȧ ɔ tǝ kǝli .
40009019	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ yi aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ yokanɛ , aŋ tȧŋ kɔ .
40009020	Ka wuni bom ulɔm ǝŋbɔwurnɛ mǝtir ta tǝren tɔfɔt tǝrǝŋ-e , ɔ der rodarǝŋ kɔŋ , ɔ gboŋ amɛsɛ ma aruma rɔŋ .
40009021	kotȧy-e ɔ pa ka ȧŋmerȧ ŋɔŋ , Bepi i gboŋ gbo aruma rɔŋ-e , i ti yeŋk .
40009022	Ma Yisɔs ɔ fǝlɛ ɔ nənk kɔ-e , ɔ , pa , Wan ka mi ubɛra , bȧk kǝbuth . Kȧlanɛ kȧmu kǝ po mu yeŋkǝs . Ka ɔwuni bom ɔ yeŋk ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati gbeŋ .
40009023	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ bek ka ȧŋseth ŋa ɔgbǝka-e , ɔ nənk aŋfɛŋ tulɛŋ yi ȧruniya aŋ bok ,
40009024	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Wur nu kotȧy-e ɔwath ubɛra ɔ fi hɛ , ɔ dirȧ gbo . Kaŋ sel kɔ bɛ .
40009025	Kɛrɛ ma a po wurɔ aŋfǝm-e , ɔ wɔŋ , kɔ wop kȧta ka ɔwath ubɛra , kɔ yokanɛ .
40009026	Ka tȧgbuŋ tati tǝ gbanthɛnɛ ka ȧŋthɔf ŋati bɛ .
40009027	Ɔwa ma Yisɔs ɔ wur ri-e , alaŋgba afith ŋarǝŋ aŋ tȧŋ kɔ , aŋ sel ɛrɔŋ kaŋ pa , Munɔ ɔwan ka Debid , ba su ȧney .
40009028	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ po wɔŋ ro seth-e , aŋlaŋgba afith aŋ der ro ŋɔŋ . Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Nǝ lanɛ kǝpa i gbǝli yɔ ȧte-i ? kaŋ wosȧnɛ kɔ , aŋ pa , Yao Pa .
40009029	kɔ gboŋ ɛfɔr yaŋ , ɔ pa , Ta pǝ yi nu mɔ mǝ kȧlanɛ ka nu kǝ yi .
40009030	Ka ɛfɔr yaŋ ɛ kanthɛ . Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ maŋ ŋa kiriŋ kiriŋ kȧmȧ aŋ te ti tɔri wuni o wuni .
40009031	Kɛrɛ maŋ wur-e , aŋ gbanthɛnɛ ȧŋes ŋɔŋ ka ȧŋthɔf ŋati bɛ .
40009032	Ɔwa maŋ wur ri-e , a kȧrȧ ulaŋgba kǝbobo ro ŋɔŋ ɔwe ba ukǝrǝfi .
40009033	Ma ɔ wurɔ ɔkǝrǝfi-e , kabobo ɔ fɔf , ka ȧruniya rǝ kabanɛ , rǝ pa , Thȧnkȧŋ a tha nənk hɛ tȧy tǝwunɔŋ kǝtɔŋ ka aŋIsrɛl .
40009034	Kɛrɛ aŋFarisi aŋ pa , Ɔ wurɔ akǝrǝfi ka kȧta ka ɔbȧy ka aŋkǝrǝfi .
40009035	Ka Yisɔs ɔ kɔth kɔth ka tapet yi ka tagbɔm bɛ , ɔ thǝksa aŋfǝm ka ɛseth yaŋ ɛgbanɛ , kɔ tamǝs ȧkɛra kǝfinɔ ka rȧbȧy , ɔ yeŋkǝs rǝtu o rǝtu ara yi kǝtɔŋ ka ŋaŋ .
40009036	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ nənk ȧsuniya-e , ȧney aŋ wop kɔ ta ȧtǝ ŋaŋ , pǝkasifɛ aŋ sɔmpanɛ , ɔwa aŋ sakanɛ mɔ tǝlɔmɛ aŋa te ba utɔl .
40009037	kɔ pa ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ karɔk kǝ yi kǝbana , kɛrɛ aŋrɔk a than .
40009038	Tiyȧŋ nɛmthɛnɛ nu ɔMarki ka karɔk , kȧmȧ ɔ somra akump ka karɔk kɔŋ .
40010001	kɔ tela ro ŋɔŋ aŋkarande ŋɔŋ tɔfɔt ŋarǝŋ , ɔ sɔŋ ŋa afɔsɔ rokɔm ka aŋkǝrǝfi alǝs tǝ kǝwura ŋa ka afǝm , dɛ yi tǝ kǝyeŋkǝs rǝtu o rǝtu .
40010002	Ɔwa ames ma aŋsom tɔfɔt ŋarǝŋ mi ame ; Ɔtɔtɔkɔ , Saymɔnȧŋ , ɔwe a bont Pita , yi ɔwɔnt kɔŋ Andru . Yemǝsȧŋ ɔwan ka Sɛbidi , dɛ yi Yɔn ɔwɔnt kɔŋ .
40010003	Filipȧŋ , Barthɔlɔmiyuȧŋ , Thɔmɔsȧŋ yi Mathyɔŋ , ɔthonkla ɛfȧk . Yemǝsȧŋ , ɔwan ka Alfiɔs , yi Thȧdiyɔsȧŋ .
40010004	Saymɔnȧŋ ɔwe ro Kenan , yi Yudas Iskariyɔt ɔwe sɔnd kɔ .
40010005	Antɔfɔt ŋarǝŋ aŋe-e , ŋa Yisɔs ɔ som , ɔ yamari ŋa , kɔ pa , Te nu kɔ ka tȧbona tǝlɔm , te nu wɔŋ rǝ kǝpet o kǝpet ka aŋSamariya ,
40010006	kɛrɛ kɔnɛ nu gbo ka talɔmɛ tǝsɔkar ta ȧŋseth ŋa aŋIsrɛl .
40010007	Ɔwa ma nǝ kɔnɛ-e , tam nu , nǝ pa , Rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ po fat .
40010008	Yenkǝs nu aŋtuy , fethǝr nu aŋa ba arom-e , yokas nu aŋfi-e , wurɔ nu aŋkǝrǝfi . Naŋ nǝ po sɔthɔ rǝ kǝte ram , ɔwa sɔŋ nu rǝ kǝte gbasi ȧrȧm .
40010009	Te nu keranɛ abɔŋɔ , akala ȧferȧ , thalɔm akɛm ka ɛbuthu ɛ nu .
40010010	Te nu keranɛ ɛgbaŋfa ka ȧŋbiyas , te nu keranɛ suma tǝrǝŋ , te nu keranɛ ɛkɔftha thalɔm tǝtǝk , kotȧy-e wuni yɔ mǝpanth ɔ mar sɔthɔ ɛyɛt yɔŋ ɛdi .
40010011	Rǝ kǝpet o kǝpet thalɔm tǝgbɔm o tǝgbɔm mȧ nǝ wɔŋ-e , thɛns ri nu wuni finɔ ; ɔwa rǝ mǝ nǝ yianɛ haŋ nǝ wur ri .
40010012	Ma nǝ wɔŋ rǝ aseth-e , kori ŋi .
40010013	Bepi ȧŋseth aŋ yi afinɔ-e , yɔ mathɔfǝl ma nu mǝ rensa ŋi , kɛrɛ bepi aŋ yi hɛ afinɔ-e , yɔ mathɔfǝl ma nu mǝ kȧl ro nu .
40010014	Ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe te malanɛ nu , ɔwa ɔ te tǝl ȧsim ta nu-e , ma nǝ wur ka ȧŋseth ŋati-e , thalɔm ka kȧpet kati-e , koŋkoŋ kabof ka ȧtȧtək ta nu .
40010015	Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , pǝ tǝ yi ɔfisa ta ȧŋthɔf ŋa ro Sɔdɔm yi ro Kɔmɔra ka ȧŋrey ŋa kagbǝk ɛpa , pǝthasi ta kȧpet kati .
40010016	Kǝla , i som nu mɔ tǝlɔmɛ kǝtɔŋ ka tȧthɔlu . Tiyȧŋ , yi nu na atempi yereŋ mɔ ɛbok , ɔwa yi nu na athɔfǝl bɛm mɔ tǝpǝrǝm .
40010017	Kɛrɛ pɛndaf nu afǝm , ȧtesoma-e aŋ tǝ lȧnki nu ka aŋgbǝka , ɔwa aŋ tǝ sapa nu nǝkɛt ka ɛseth yaŋ ɛgbanɛ .
40010018	Aŋ tǝ kera nu sɔ rodi ka aŋbȧy yi aŋbȧki salata mi , kȧmȧ nǝ yi mǝseri ro ŋaŋ yi ka tȧbona tǝlɔm .
40010019	Kɛrɛ ma a lȧnki nu-e , te nu soli ta ȧte mǝ nǝ fɔf , kotȧy-e ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati a tǝ sɔŋ nu ȧte mǝ nǝ fɔf .
40010020	kotȧy-e naŋ tha mǝ fɔf , kɛrɛ ɔYina mǝsǝm ka ɔKas ka nu kɔnɔ mǝ fɔf rokor ka nu .
40010021	Ɔwɔnt ɔ tǝ lȧnki ɔwɔnt ka rǝfi , ɔwa ɔkas ɔ tǝ lȧnki ɔwan kɔŋ . Ɔwa awuth aŋ tǝ yokar aŋa kom ŋa kȧmȧ aŋ yɔ a dif ŋa .
40010022	Afǝm bɛ aŋ tǝ gbɛŋa nu salata ȧŋes a mi , kɛrɛ ɔwe mǝ muyu haŋ ka ɔthalnɛ-e , kɔnɔ kati ɔ tǝ kisi .
40010023	Bepi a sompa nu ka kȧpet ake-e , gbukɛ nu nǝ kɔ ka kȧlɔm . Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , nǝ gbǝli hɛ po kori tapet ta aŋIsrɛl bɛ haŋ ɔWan ka wuni ɔ po der .
40010024	Ukarande ɔ thas hɛ ɔkarmɔkɔ kɔŋ , thalɔm ȧbɔy ɔ thas hɛ ɔmarki kɔŋ .
40010025	Ɔbeki ta ɔkarande tǝ kǝyi mɔ ɔkarmɔkɔ kɔŋ , dɛ yi ȧŋbɔy mɔ ɔmarki kɔŋ . Bepi a po bont ɔmarki kɔŋ , dɛ yi ȧŋbɔy mɔ ɔmarki kɔŋ . Bepi a po bont ɔmarki ka ȧŋseth Biyɛlsibɔb-e , pǝ tha gbethi ŋaŋ aŋa yi ka kabɔr kɔŋ .
40010026	Tiyȧŋ te nu nesa ŋa , kotȧy-e tȧy tǝgbǝpǝr tǝ yi hɛ ȧte mǝ a te ba kǝgbǝpǝri ; ɔwa tȧy tǝmaŋknɛ tǝ yi hɛ ȧte mǝ a te ba kǝŋaibi .
40010027	Ȧtȧ i kanɛ nu ka ɔbi-e , pa ti nu ka ɔwaŋ . Ɔwa ȧte nǝ tǝl ro lǝns-e , tam ti nu ka ɛseth rokɔm .
40010028	Te nesa aŋa mǝ dif aŋdɛr , kɛrɛ aŋ gbǝli hɛ dif aŋesǝm . Kɛrɛ nesa nu kɔn ɔwe gbǝli dim aŋesǝm dɛ yi aŋdɛr ro yahanama .
40010029	A thila hɛ ɛgbaŋa ŋarǝŋ ta apɛni-i ? Ɔwa hali ukin ka ŋaŋ ɔ fumpɔ hɛ ro thɔf thambe ɔKas ka nu ɔ tȧrȧ ti .
40010030	Ɔwa hali aŋfon ŋa tabomp ta nu-e , a po lɔm ŋa bɛ .
40010031	Tiyȧŋ te nu nesa , nǝ ba mɔlɔ pǝthasi ɛgbaŋa agbȧthi .
40010032	Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ seri ta ȧta mi rodi ka aŋfǝm , minɛ sɔ i ti seri ta atɔŋ rodi ka ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40010033	Kɛrɛ wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ pɛnsanɛ mi rodi ka aŋfǝm-e , minɛ sɔ i ti pɛnsanɛ kɔ rodi ka ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40010034	Te nanɛ kǝpa i der tǝ kǝsɔŋ mǝthɔfǝl ka ȧdȧru . I der hɛ tǝ kǝsɔŋ mǝthɔfǝl , kɛrɛ i karanɛ agbathɔ .
40010035	kotȧy-e i der tǝ kǝbot mǝputhanɛ kǝtɔŋ ka ɔwan uruni yi ɔkas kɔŋ , kǝtɔŋ ka ɔwan ubɛra yi ɔkara kɔŋ , dɛ yi kǝtɔŋ ka ɔwe balȧ ka ɔwan kɔŋ uruni yi ɔniŋkara kɔŋ .
40010036	Ɔwa aŋtheranɛ ŋa wuni aŋ tǝ yi ka rȧkomra rɔŋ gbeŋ .
40010037	Wuni o wuni ɔwe bɔthǝr ɔkas thalɔm ɔkara pǝthasi minɛȧŋ , ɔ bek hɛ ta ȧtȧ mi . Ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe bɔthǝr ɔwan uruni thalɔm ɔwan ubɛra pǝthasi minɛȧŋ , ɔ bek hɛ ta ȧtȧ mi .
40010038	Ɔwa kɔn ɔwe te gbasi akǝnt kɔŋ kǝpǝŋkinɛ , ɔ tȧŋ mi-e , ɔ bek hɛ ta ȧtȧ mi
40010039	Ɔwe mǝ bɛnɛ aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ ɔ tǝ dim ŋi , ɔwa ɔwe mǝ dim aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ salata mi ɔ tǝ fir ŋi .
40010040	Ɔwe malanɛ nu ɔ malanɛ mi , ɔwa ɔwe malanɛ mi-e , ɔ malanɛ ɔwe som mi .
40010041	Ɔwe mǝ malanɛ unabi pǝkasifɛ ɔ yi unabi-e , ɔ tǝ sɔthɔ ȧŋrȧm ŋa unabi , ɔwa ɔwe mǝ malanɛ wuni lompi pǝkasifɛ ɔ yi wuni lompi-e , ɔ tǝ sɔthɔ ȧŋrȧm ŋa wuni lompi .
40010042	Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ sɔŋ apɔthi ŋa mȧnt mǝtaŋk tǝ kǝmun ka ukin ka aŋlɔl aŋe pǝkasifɛ ɔ yi ukarande-e , i kanɛ nu tɛntɛnɛ ɔ ba hɛ kǝdim ȧŋrȧm ŋɔŋ .
40011001	Ka pǝ re yi ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ po yamari aŋkarande ŋɔŋ tɔfɔt ŋarǝŋ-e , ɔ wur ri tǝ kǝthǝksa dɛ yi tǝ kǝtam ka tapet taŋ .
40011002	Ma Yɔnȧŋ ɔ tǝl ka ȧŋseth ŋa tȧrǝŋka mȧyɔs ma Kraist-e , ɔ som akarande ŋɔŋ ŋarǝŋ .
40011003	kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Munɔ yi kɔn ɔwe ba kǝder-i , thalɔm sǝ ba tǝ kǝkǝli ta ulɔm-i ?
40011004	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ lasi ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Kɔnɛ nǝ tɔri Yɔn mȧtȧy ama nǝ tǝl dɛ yi ama nǝ nənk .
40011005	Aŋfith aŋ sɔthɔ kakǝli ka ŋaŋ , aŋtǝtkɛ aŋ kɔth , aŋa ba rǝlel-e , a fethǝr ŋa , aŋtȧŋȧ aŋ tǝl , a yokas aŋfi-e , ɔwa a tɔri ȧkɛra kǝfinɔ ka Kuru ka ȧŋmɔnɛ .
40011006	Ɔwa wuni ka aruba wɔŋ ɔwe te fir tȧy tǝpǝnthbǝla ro rɔmi .
40011007	Maŋ po kɔnɛ-e , Yisɔs ɔ tǝp kǝpa ka ȧsuniya ta salata Yɔn , Ko tȧy tȧŋ nǝ kɔ ro wula tǝ kǝkǝli-e ? Kǝthȧŋkɛ ȧke aŋfef aŋ yinktha-i ?
40011008	Kɛrɛ ko tȧy tȧŋ nǝ wur tǝ kǝkǝli-e ? Wuni ɔwe lopra ɛlopra ɛnɔfthɔ-i ? Kǝla , ŋaŋ aŋa wɔŋ ɛlopra ɛnɔfthɔ aŋ yi ka ɛseth ya aŋbȧy .
40011009	Kɛrɛ kɔyɛŋ gbeŋ nǝ wur-e ? Tǝ kǝnǝŋk unabi-i ? Aŋko i kanɛ nu-e , uthasi unabi .
40011010	Kɔn ɔwe ta ɔwe a gbal kǝpa , Kǝla i som ɔsom kȧmi roder ka mu kǝdi , Ɔwe mǝ bɛmpa aroŋ da mu rodi kȧmu .
40011011	Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , kǝtɔŋ ka ŋaŋ aŋa afǝm abom aŋ kom wuni ɔ tha yokanɛ hɛ ɔwe yi ubana uthasi Yɔnȧŋ ɔBaftays . Kɛrɛ ɔwe yi ɔlɔl thɔŋ bɛ ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana ɔ yi ubana uthasi kɔ .
40011012	Kǝtǝp ka mȧrey ma Yɔn ɔBaftays haŋ ka ȧŋlɔkɔ aŋe rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ tǝlnɛ afɔsɔ-e , ɔwa aŋfǝm ŋa afɔsɔ aŋ gbasi ŋi rǝ afɔsɔ .
40011013	kotȧy-e aŋnabi yi aŋthɔ aŋ nȧbi haŋ ka kȧder ka Yɔn .
40011014	Ɔwa bepi nǝ selɔ tǝ kǝmalanɛ ti-e , Ilaya kɔn ɔwe , ɔwe ba tǝ kǝder .
40011015	Ɔwe ba ɛlǝns ta ɔ tǝl .
40011016	Ko rǝka raŋ mǝ i lomɔ rȧkomra are-e ? Rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ afɛth aŋa yirȧ ka ɔdɛr ɔthila , aŋ muti aŋkos ŋaŋ ,
40011017	kaŋ pa , Sǝ fɛŋa nu tulɛŋ , nǝ thɔmɔ hɛ ; sǝ leŋa nu mǝleŋ ma rǝbora , kɛrɛ nǝ bok hɛ .
40011018	kotȧy-e Yɔnȧŋ ɔ der hɛ rǝ kǝdi thalɔm rǝ kǝmun , kaŋ pa , Ɔ ba ukǝrǝfi .
40011019	ƆWan ka wuni ɔ der rǝ kǝdi dɛ yi rǝ kǝmun , ɔwa aŋ pa , Kǝli ulaŋgba uwɔnthi rɛ umun ubana-e , uyathki ka aŋthoŋkla ɛfȧk yi aŋfǝm ŋa ɛhakɛ . Kɛrɛ kǝtemp kǝ tǝ sɔthɔ mǝmari ka mȧyɔs mati .
40011020	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati ɔ tǝp kǝthɛkɛ tapet ro ɔ tha po yɔ mȧyɔs mɔŋ mǝkabanɛ , pǝkasifɛ aŋ thupi hɛ , kɔ pa ,
40011021	Mɔnɛ ro mu Korasin ! Mɔnɛ ro mu Bɛthsayda ! kotȧy-e bepi mȧyɔs mǝkabanɛ ama a po yɔ kǝtɔŋ ka nu-e , a yɔ ma naŋ ro Tair dɛ yi ro Sidon-e , aŋ tǝ po naŋ thupi ɔwoni rǝ kotha kǝnɛthɛ dɛ yi rǝ ros .
40011022	Kɛrɛ i kanɛ nu , pǝ tǝ yi ɔfisa ta ro Tair yi ro Sidon ka ȧŋrey ŋa kǝthoŋkas pǝthasi nu .
40011023	Ɔwa munɔ Kepaniyɔm , a tǝ ŋata mu ro riana-i ? A tǝ thora mu ro kǝrǝfi ! kotȧy-e bepi aŋ po naŋ yɔ mȧyɔs mǝkabanɛ ro Sɔdɔm ama a po yɔ ro mu-e , kǝ tǝ tǝma naŋ haŋ ka-ake .
40011024	Kɛrɛ i kanɛ nu , pǝ tǝ yi ɔfisa ta ȧŋthɔf ŋa ro Sɔdɔm ka ȧŋrey ŋa kǝthoŋkas pǝthasi munɔ .
40011025	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa , I mɔmɔ mu , ɔKas ɔMarki ka ro riyana yi ȧdȧru , pǝkasifɛ mǝ po maŋk mȧtȧy ame ka aŋtempi yi aŋtara tȧy , ɔwa mǝ ŋaibi ma ka tǝlɛnth .
40011026	Aŋko , ɔKas , ȧtesoma-e ya pǝ yi ɔfinɔ ka kakǝli ka mu .
40011027	ƆKas kȧmi ɔ po sɔŋ mi mətȧy bɛ , ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔ tɛ hɛ ɔWan thambe ɔKas ; ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔ tɛ hɛ ɔKas thambe ɔWan dɛ yi ka ɔwe ɔWan ɔ yema tǝ kǝŋaibi kɔ .
40011028	Der nu ro rɔmi , naŋ bɛ aŋa mǝ thɔrɔ dɛ yi aŋa ba tothe tǝlel , ɔwa i ti sɔŋ nu kǝfothanɛ .
40011029	Gbasi kȧronke kȧmi nǝ rǝnȧ ki , kȧmȧ nǝ thǝkǝs ro rɔmi ; kotȧy-e min thɔfǝl bɛm , i kȧl ba ȧmerȧ athoranɛ , ɔwa nǝ tǝ fir kǝfothanɛ ka ɛŋesǝm ɛ nu .
40011030	kotȧy-e kȧronke kȧmi kǝ tui hɛ tȧy , ɔwa akothe kȧmi kǝ fǝŋf .
40012001	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ gbǝkinɛ atɔr ka aŋsabath . Ɔwa ma aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ yi ador-e , aŋ tǝp kǝsimǝth magbas , kaŋ di ma .
40012002	Kɛrɛ ma aŋFarisi aŋ nənk ti-e , aŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Kǝli aŋkarande a mu aŋ yɔ ȧte pǝ te mar yɔ ka ȧŋrey ŋa aŋsabath .
40012003	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Nǝ tha karaŋ hɛ ȧte Debid ɔ yɔ ma dor rǝ bȧk kɔ dɛ yi ŋaŋ aŋa yi yi kɔn-i ?
40012004	Ma ɔ wɔŋ ka ȧŋseth ŋa Kuru , kɔ di kabo kǝsǝm ȧke pǝ te mar di ta atɔŋ thalɔm ta ȧte ŋaŋ aŋa yi yi kɔnɔ , thambe gbo ta aŋfode-i ?
40012005	Thalɔm nǝ tha karaŋ hɛ ka aŋthɔ kǝpa ka aŋsabath aŋfode ŋa ȧŋseth ŋa Kuru aŋ lǝsǝr aŋsabath , kɛrɛ aŋ ba hɛ mǝthɛkɛ-i ?
40012006	Kɛrɛ i kanɛ nu kǝpa , ukin ɔwe yi ubana pǝthasi ȧŋseth ŋa Kuru ɔ yi nɔ .
40012007	Ɔwa bepi nǝ tȧrȧ naŋ aŋlokthi ŋa ȧsim ȧte , I fela ȧney , pǝ yi hɛ sathka , nǝ gbǝli hɛ naŋ sɔŋ mǝtheri ka ŋaŋ aŋa yi apaŋi tȧy .
40012008	kotȧy-e ɔWan ka wuni ɔ yi ɔMarki ka aŋsabath .
40012009	Ma ɔ wur ri-e , ɔ kɔnɛ ka ȧŋseth ŋaŋ agbanɛ .
40012010	Ka wuni ɔ yi ri ɔwe ba kǝta kǝfi . Kaŋ yif kɔ , aŋ pa , Pǝ yi ɔlompi tǝ kǝyeŋkǝs wuni ka ȧŋrey ŋa ȧŋsabath-i ? ( kȧmȧ aŋ ba tȧy tǝ kǝgbanthir kɔ ) .
40012011	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Wuni reke kǝtɔŋ ka nu ɔwe mǝ ba kǝlɔmɛ kin , bepi ɔ fumpɔ rǝ abi ka aŋsabath-e , mǝ ɔ te wop kɔ tǝ kǝwura kɔ-e ?
40012012	Thamsinɛ wuni kǝpet ɔ ba amɔlɔ pǝthasi kǝlɔmɛ ! Tiyȧŋ pǝ yi ɔlompi tǝ kǝyɔ tȧy tǝfinɔ ka ȧŋrey ŋa aŋsabath .
40012013	kɔ pa ka ɔlaŋgba , Thanthi kȧta ka mu . Kɔ thanthi ki , ka kǝ kȧl yeŋk mɔ kalɔm .
40012014	Ka aŋFarisi aŋ wur , aŋ nǝŋkanɛ ta atɔŋ , to mǝ aŋ yɔ tǝ kǝdif kɔ .
40012015	Yisɔsȧŋ ma ɔ tȧrȧ ti-e , ɔ wur ri , ka agbȧthi aŋ tȧŋ kɔ , kɔ yeŋkǝs ŋa bɛ .
40012016	Kɛrɛ ɔ maŋ ŋa kȧmȧ aŋ te yɔ a tȧrȧ kɔ ,
40012017	kȧmȧ ȧte Isaya ɔnȧbi ɔ pa tǝ lasǝr , kǝpa ,
40012018	Kǝla , ȧŋbɔy a mi ɔwe i po thith , Ɔbɔthǝr kȧmi ka ɔwe ȧŋmerȧ a mi aŋ ba mǝbɔnɛ . I ti bot ɔYina kȧmi ro ŋɔŋ , Ɔwa ɔ tǝ tɔri mǝlompi ka tȧbona tǝlɔm .
40012019	Ɔ ba hɛ kǝgbȧl , thalɔm kǝŋȧtȧ ȧrim rɔŋ , Ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔ ba hɛ kǝtǝl ȧrim rɔŋ ka asoŋ tǝbana .
40012020	Ɔ ba hɛ kǝsim kǝthȧnkɛ kǝnulȧ , Ɔ ba hɛ kǝdimsi awik aŋa mǝ wur kimȧ , Haŋ ɔ somrȧ kǝthoŋkas tǝ kǝtham .
40012021	Ɔwa ka ȧŋes ŋɔŋ tȧbona tǝlɔm tǝ tǝ gbak ȧmerȧ .
40012022	kaŋ kȧrȧ wuni ɔwe ba ukǝrǝfi ro ŋɔŋ , ɔ yi ufith dɛ yi kǝbobo . Kɔ yeŋkǝs kɔ , ɔwa ɔlaŋgba kǝbobo ɔ nənk , ɔ kȧl fɔf .
40012023	Ka ȧsuniya bɛ aŋ kabanɛ , aŋ pa , ƆWan ka Debid , kɔn tha ɔwe-i ?
40012024	Kɛrɛ ma aŋFarisi aŋ tǝl ti-e , aŋ pa , Ɔwuni ɔwe ɔ wurɔ akǝrǝfi ka aŋfɔsɔ ŋa Biyɛlsibɔb , ɔbȧy ka aŋkǝrǝfi .
40012025	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tȧrȧ ɛnanɛ yaŋ-e , ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Rǝbai o rǝbai ro mǝputhanɛ mǝ wɔŋ rǝ tǝ sakthɛ ; ɔwa kǝpet o kǝpet thalɔm aseth o seth ro mǝputhanɛ mǝ yi aŋ gbǝli hɛ tǝma .
40012026	Bepi Sethani ɔ wurɔ Sethani-e , ɔ timnɛ , ɔwa to rȧbȧy rɔŋ mǝ rǝ gbǝli tǝma-e ?
40012027	Bepi i wurɔ akǝrǝfi ka aŋfɔsɔ ŋa Biyɛlsibɔbȧŋ , rǝ kȧta ka kanɛ aŋwuth a nu mǝ aŋ wurɔ ŋa-e ? Tiyȧŋ ŋa mǝ gbǝka nu ȧŋpa .
40012028	Kɛrɛ bepi i wurɔ akǝrǝfi ka aŋfɔsɔ ŋa ɔYina ka Kuru Mǝsaba-e , rȧbȧy ra Kuru rǝ derǝr nu .
40012029	Thalɔm to wuni mǝ ɔ gbǝli wɔŋ rǝ ȧŋseth ŋa wuni ba afɔsɔ tǝ kǝlukǝs ɛyɛt yɔŋ thambe ɔ mɔtha sek ɔwuni kati-e ? Kǝdarǝŋ kati ɔ tǝ gbǝli tɛn lukǝs ɛyɛt ya ȧŋseth ŋɔŋ .
40012030	Ɔwe te yi ka ȧŋgbȧp a mi ɔ tǝma kǝŋamnɛ mi . Ɔwe te thoŋkla dɛ yi minɛȧŋ , ɔ sakthi .
40012031	Tiyȧŋ i kanɛ nu , ɛhakɛ bɛ-e , dɛ yi ȧsim tǝlǝs bɛ ȧte afǝm mǝ aŋ fɔf kǝŋamnɛ Kuruȧŋ , a tǝ tera ŋa ti , kɛrɛ a ba hɛ kǝtera ɔwuni ɔwe mǝ fɔf kǝŋamnɛ ɔYina mǝsǝm .
40012032	Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ fɔf ɔlǝs ta ɔWan ka wuni , a tǝ tera kɔ ti ; kɛrɛ ɔwe mǝ fɔf ɔlǝs ta ɔYina mǝsǝm , a ba hɛ kǝtera kɔ ti hali ka ȧdȧru are , ta a pa ras ka ȧdȧru ara mǝ derȧŋ .
40012033	Yɔ hɔ kȧmȧ aŋǝnt aŋ thesa , yi mȧkomi mati mǝ thesa , thalɔm yɔ aŋǝnt aŋ lǝsǝ yi mȧkomi mati mǝ lǝsǝ ; kotȧy-e a tȧrȧ aŋǝnt ka mȧkomi mati .
40012034	Naŋ rǝkomra ra ɛgbɔrɔ , to mǝ nǝ gbǝli fɔf mətȧy mǝfinɔ ma nǝ yi alǝs-e ? kotȧy-e kasǝŋ kǝ tǝ fɔf kǝwur ka kala ka ȧŋmerȧ .
40012035	Ɔwuni finɔ ɔ wurɔ mətȧy mǝfinɔ ka ɛbɛnɛnɛ yɔŋ ɛfinɔ , ɔwa ɔwuni lǝs ɔ wurɔ mətȧy mǝlɔs ka ɛbɛnɛnɛ yɔŋ ɛlǝs .
40012036	Kɛrɛ i kanɛ nu kǝpa-e , rim o rim rǝyai ara afǝm mǝ aŋ fɔf aŋ ba tǝ kǝgbaki ti ka ȧŋrey ŋa kǝthoŋkas .
40012037	kotȧy-e ka ȧsim ta mu rǝ mǝ a sɔŋ mu mǝmari , ɔwa ka ȧsim ta mu rǝ mǝ a sɔŋ mu mǝtheri .
40012038	Ka aŋkarmɔkɔ dɛ yi aŋFarisi alɔm aŋ pa , Karmɔkɔ , sǝ yema nənk amisali ka kȧta ka mu .
40012039	Kɛrɛ ɔ wosa ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Rǝkomra rǝlǝs , rǝte lanɛ rǝ thɛns amisali , kɛrɛ a sɔŋ hɛ ŋa amisali , thambe ȧŋmisali ŋa ɔnȧbi Yona .
40012040	kotȧy-e mɔ mǝ Yonaȧŋ ɔ ba mǝrei mǝsas pali gbɛs ka akor ka kalop kǝbana-e , ya ɔWan ka wuni mǝ ɔ yi rokor ka ȧŋthɔf mǝrei mǝsas pali gbɛsȧŋ .
40012041	Aŋfǝm ŋa ro Ninifɛ aŋ tǝ tǝma yi rȧkomra are ka kathoŋkas-e , aŋ tǝ sɔŋ ri mǝtheri , kotȧy-e aŋ thupi ka kakawandi ka Yona , ɔwe yi ubana uthasi Yonaȧŋ ɔ yi nɔ .
40012042	Ɔbȧy ubɛra ka ȧŋthɔf ȧdiyɔ ɔ tǝ yokanɛ yi rȧkomra are ka kathoŋkas-e , ɔ tǝ sɔŋ ri mǝtheri , kotȧy-e ɔ wur ɔbɔli tǝ kǝtǝl kȧtemp ka Sɔlɔmɔn , ɔwe yi ubana uthasi Sɔlɔmɔn ɔ yi nɔ .
40012043	Ma ɔkǝrǝfi ulǝs ɔ wur ka wuni-e , ɔ yanta yanta dɛr ro mȧnt mǝ te yi , ɔ thɛns kǝfothanɛ kɛrɛ ɔ fir hɛ ki .
40012044	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati ɔ tǝ pa , I ti kȧlanɛ ka ȧŋseth a mi ro i wur . Ma ɔ bek ri-e , ɔ fir ŋi afoth , agbǝl , ɔwa ayesi .
40012045	Ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati ɔ kɔnɛ , ɔ karanɛ akǝrǝfi tamthǝdɛrǝŋ alɔm aŋa yi alǝs athasi kɔ , kaŋ wɔŋ aŋ yirȧ ri . Ɔwa mȧlǝpsɔ ma ɔwuni kati mǝ yi mǝlǝs mǝthasi matɔtɔkɔ . Ya pǝ yi sɔ yi rȧkomra rǝlǝs are .
40012046	Ma ɔ bɔ fɔfȧnɛ aŋfǝm-e , ɔkara kɔŋ yi aŋwɔnt ŋɔŋ aŋ tǝma rokaŋ , aŋ yema kǝ fɔfȧnɛ kɔ .
40012047	Ka ukin ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Ɔya ka mu yi aŋwɔnt mu aŋ tǝma rokaŋ , aŋ yema kǝfɔfanɛ mu .
40012048	Kɛrɛ ɔ lasi , ɔ pa ka ɔwe kanɛ kɔ-e , Kanɛ yi ɔkara ka mi-e , ɔwa kanɛ ŋaŋ yi aŋwɔnt a mi-e ?
40012049	kɔ thanthi kȧta kɔŋ , ɔ lomanɛ ki ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , kɔ pa , Kǝli ɔkara kȧmi dɛ yi aŋwɔnt a mi !
40012050	Ȧtesoma-e wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ yɔ mȧselɔ ma ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riana-e , kɔnɔ yi ɔwɔnt mi uruni yi ɔwɔnt mi ubɛra dɛ yi ɔkara kȧmi .
40013001	Ka ȧŋrey ŋati Yisɔs ɔ wur ka ȧŋseth , ɔ kɔ yirȧ ro baŋ rayɛr .
40013002	Ka suniya tǝbana tǝ thoŋklanɛ ro ŋɔŋ , haŋ ɔ wɔŋ ka abil , ɔ yirȧ . Ka ȧruniya bɛ rǝ tǝma ro gbaŋ .
40013003	kɔ fɔfȧnɛ ŋa mətȧy mǝgbathi rǝ ɛlomɔ , ɔ pa , Kǝla , usak ɔ wur tǝ kǝsak .
40013004	Ma ɔ sak-e , mater mǝlɔm mǝ fumpɔ ro roŋ dayɛr , ka ɛbȧmp aŋ der aŋ gbȧmǝs ma .
40013005	Mǝlɔm mǝ fumpɔ rǝ agbalaŋ , ro mǝ te ba ɛthɔf ɛgbathi . Ɔlɛmp gbo mǝ lɔkɔ-e , ȧtesoma-e mǝ ba hɛ ɛthɔf ɛbɔlɔŋ .
40013006	Ɔwa ma aret rǝ gbep-e , ȧney nǝ gbaŋar ma , mǝ wela pǝkasifɛ mǝ ba hɛ ɛthǝnk .
40013007	Mǝlɔm mǝ fumpɔ ka tȧbȧnk ratɔŋ , ka tȧbȧnk tǝ lɔkɔ , tǝ thiŋkanɛ ma .
40013008	Kɛrɛ mǝlɔm mǝ fumpɔ ka ȧŋthɔf afinɔ , ka mǝ kom mǝkomi , mǝlɔm mɔlɔ ma kɛmɛ kin , mǝlɔm tǝgba tǝsas , mǝlɔm kǝgba tɔfɔt .
40013009	Ɔwe ba ɛlǝns ta ɔ tǝl .
40013010	Ka aŋkarande aŋ der aŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , To pǝ som mǝ fɔfȧnɛ ŋa rǝ ɛlomɔ-e ?
40013011	kɔ lasi ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Ro rɔnu a sɔŋ kȧtȧrȧ ka ɛgbundu ya rȧbȧy ra ro riyana , kɛrɛ ro rɔŋaŋ a sɔŋ hɛ ki .
40013012	kotȧy-e wuni o wuni ɔwe ba , kɔnɔ mǝ a sɔŋ , ɔ tǝ ba agbȧthi , kɛrɛ wuni o wuni ɔwe te ba , a tǝ nɔy kɔ hali ara ɔ ba .
40013013	Tȧsom i fɔfȧnɛ ŋa rǝ ɛlomɔ , pǝkasifɛ hali aŋ kǝli aŋ nənk hɛ , ɔwa hali aŋ su ɛlǝns aŋ tǝl hɛ , ɔwa pǝ sɔk hɛ ŋa .
40013014	A lasǝr tapa ta Isaya ro rɔŋaŋ , ȧte pa ye , Rǝ kǝsu ɛlǝns nǝ tǝ tǝl , kɛrɛ pǝ gbǝli hɛ sɔk nu , Rǝ kǝkǝli nǝ tǝ nənk , kɛrɛ nǝ gbǝli hɛ gbɛnthas ti .
40013015	kotȧy-e ɛmerȧ ya aŋfǝm aŋe ɛ gbolŋanɛ , Ɔwa ɛlǝns yaŋ ɛ tui tǝl , Ɔwa aŋ po mɔp ɛfɔr yaŋ , Ta thani aŋ ti nənk yi ɛfɔr yaŋ , Ɔwa aŋ tǝl yi ɛlǝns yaŋ , Pǝ tǝ kȧl sɔk ŋa rǝ ȧmerȧ , Ɔwa aŋ kȧl lafthɛ Kama , i yeŋkǝs ŋa .
40013016	Kɛrɛ ɛfɔr ɛ nu ɛ ba aruba , ȧtesoma-e ɛ nənk , dɛ yi ɛlǝns ɛ nu sɔ , ȧtesoma-e ɛ tǝl .
40013017	Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu-e , anȧbi yi afǝm alompi agbȧthi aŋ fela tǝ kǝnǝŋk mȧtȧy ama naŋ nǝ nənk kɛrɛ aŋ nənk hɛ ma : dɛ yi tǝ kǝtǝl mȧtȧy ama naŋ nǝ tǝl , kɛrɛ aŋ tǝl hɛ ma .
40013018	I ti lokthɛ nu ȧŋlomɔ ŋa ɔsak .
40013019	Bepi wuni o wuni ɔ tǝl ȧrim ra rabȧy-e , ɔwa pǝ sɔk hɛ kɔ-e , Sethani ɔ der , ɔ kathi kɔ ȧte a po sak ka ȧŋmerȧ ŋɔŋ . Ɔwe-e , kɔnɔ a sak ro roŋ dayɛr .
40013020	Kɛrɛ kɔnɔ ɔwe a sak ka aŋgbalaŋ-e , kɔnɔ yi ɔwe mǝ tǝl ȧrim yi mǝbɔnɛ , ɔwa ɔ malanɛ ri .
40013021	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ te ba athǝnk-e , ɔ tǝma gbo ta alɔkɔ agbut . Ɔwa ma mɔnɛ thalɔm asɔmpanɛ aŋ bek salata ȧrim , lɛmp ɔ tǝ pǝnthbǝla .
40013022	Ɔwa kɔnɔ ɔwe a sak ka tabaŋk ratɔŋ-e , kɔnɔ yi ɔwe mǝ tǝl ȧrim , kɛrɛ aŋsoli ŋa ȧdȧru yi matɔns ma rȧyola mǝ tɔkǝr ȧrim , ɔwa ɔ kom hɛ sɔ mǝkomi .
40013023	Kɛrɛ kɔnɔ ɔwe a sak ka ȧŋthɔf afinɔ ɔ yi kɔnɔ ɔwe mǝ tǝl ȧrim , ɔwa pǝ sɔk kɔ . Ɔ kom mǝkomi tɛntɛnɛ , kɔ kom mǝlɔm mɔlɔ ma kɛmɛ kin , mǝlɔm mɔlɔ ma tǝgba tǝsas , mǝlɔm mɔlɔ ma kǝgba tɔfɔt .
40013024	kɔ bot alomɔ alɔm rodi ka ŋaŋ , ɔ pa , Rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ wuni ɔwe sak mǝter mǝfinɔ ka akɔr kɔŋ ,
40013025	kɛrɛ ka tatak-e , ɔtheranɛ kɔŋ ɔ der ɔ sak kǝpika kǝtɔŋ apǝla , kɔ kɔnɛ .
40013026	Ɔwa ma mǝ lɔkɔ-e , mǝ wur ɛgbas-e , kapika sɔ kǝ wurnɛ .
40013027	Ka ɛbɔy ya ɔkas ka ȧŋseth aŋ der aŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Pa , mǝter mǝfinɔ tha mǝ sak ro kɔr kamu-i ? To pǝ tǝp kǝpika kǝ yi ri-e ?
40013028	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Utheranɛ ulɔm kɔnɔ po yɔ ȧte . Ka ɛbɔy aŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Mǝ yema sǝ kɔ tusi kapika-i ?
40013029	Kɛrɛ ɔ pa , Sako , ta thani bepi nǝ tusi kapika-e , nǝ tǝ tusianɛ sɔ apǝla .
40013030	Ter yi yɛrǝŋȧŋ ɛ lɔkɔ dɛr ɔkin haŋ ka karɔk , ɔwa ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋa karɔk i ti pa ka aŋrɔk , Mɔtha nu thoŋkla kapika , ɔwa sekǝth ki rǝ ɛlik tǝ kǝthɔy . Kɛrɛ thoŋkla apǝla pa mi ro fuŋk .
40013031	kɔ bot sɔ alomɔ alɔm rodi ka ŋaŋ , ɔ pa , Rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ aluka ŋa amustard aŋa wuni ɔ gbasi , ɔ tɛp ka akɔr kɔŋ .
40013032	Aŋ yi alɔl athasi maluka bɛ , kɛrɛ bepi aŋ po bȧk-e , aŋ yi ȧbana athasi ɛbuma bɛ , aŋ sǝkɛ ŋǝnt , ɔwa ɛbȧmp ya aŋfena aŋ der , kaŋ seth ka mara mati .
40013033	kɔ fɔf sɔ alomɔ alɔm ro ŋaŋ , ɔ pa , Rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ ɛgbith ɛyɛ wuni bom ɔ gbasi ɔ maŋk rǝ rɛkɛ ra ɛthunth ɛsas , haŋ yi bɛ ɛ sǝkɛ ɛgbith .
40013034	Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ fɔf mȧtȧy ame bɛ ka ȧsuniya rǝ ɛlomɔ , ɔwa ɔ fɔfȧnɛ hɛ ŋa koko pǝthas rǝ alomɔ ,
40013035	kȧmȧ ȧrim ra ɔnȧbi rǝ lasǝr ara pa , I ti fɔf rǝ ɛlomɔ , I ti thǝksa mȧtȧy ama a maŋk rǝ agbundu kǝbi ka ɔtɔpɛr wa ȧdȧru .
40013036	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tey ȧsuniya-e , ɔ wɔŋ ro seth , ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ der ro ŋɔŋ aŋ pa , Lokthia su aŋlomɔ ŋa kapika ro kɔr .
40013037	kɔ wosa , ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Ɔwe sak mater mǝfinɔ kɔnɔ yi ɔWan ka wuni .
40013038	Ɔwa akɔr-e , kǝ yi ȧdȧru . Mater mǝfinɔ mǝ yi aŋwuth ŋa rȧbȧy , kɛrɛ kapika kǝ yi aŋwuth ŋa ɔwuni lǝs .
40013039	Ɔtheranɛ ɔwe sak ki-e , Sethani kɔnɔȧŋ . Ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋa karɔk aŋ yi ɔthalnɛ wa ȧdȧru , ɔwa aŋrɔk , ŋa yi aŋmȧleka .
40013040	Tiyȧŋ mɔ mǝ a thoŋkla kapika , ɔwa a thɔi ki ro nant-e , ya mǝ pǝ yi ka ɔthalnɛ wa ȧdȧru .
40013041	ƆWan ka wuni ɔ ba kǝsom aŋmȧleka ŋɔŋ kȧmȧ aŋ wurɔ ka rȧbȧy rɔŋ matȧy bɛ ama sɔŋ kǝyɛthȧ , dɛ yi ŋaŋ aŋa yɔ ɔlǝs .
40013042	Ɔwa a tǝ fitha ŋa rǝ atoŋ ŋa nȧnt ro kǝkulɔ yi kȧŋȧkŋȧk ɛsek kǝ yi .
40013043	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati aŋlompi aŋ tǝ gbɛntha mɔ aret ka rȧbȧy ra ɔKas ka ŋaŋ . Ɔwe ba ɛlǝns ta ɔ tǝl .
40013044	Rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ kɛŋ kǝbaki mɔlɔ ȧke a maŋk ro lal , ȧke wuni ɔ fir , ɔ kȧl maŋk ki , ɔwa ɔ kɔnɛ ɔ thila ara ɔ ba bɛ salata mabɔnɛ mati , kȧmȧ ɔ gbǝli wai aŋlal ŋati .
40013045	Ɔwa sɔ-e , rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ wuni sǝkinɛ ɔwe thɛns mǝsar mǝbaki mɔlɔ .
40013046	Ɔwa ma ɔ po fir ȧsar ŋin abȧki mɔlɔ-e , ɔ kɔ thila ara ɔ ba bɛ-e , kȧmȧ ɔ wai ŋi .
40013047	Ɔwa rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ sɔ mɔ kǝpɛl kǝgboya ȧke a fak ro baŋ , ɔwa kǝ gbip ɛlop agbaskɛ gbaskɛ .
40013048	Ma kǝ po la-e , a liŋ ki ro gbaŋ , kaŋ yirȧ aŋ thoŋkla aŋfinɔ rǝ tǝbǝlai , kaŋ fitha aŋlǝs .
40013049	Ya mǝ pǝ yi ka ɔthalnɛ wa ȧdȧru . Aŋmȧleka aŋ tǝ der , aŋ tǝ gbaski aŋlǝs ka aŋlompi ,
40013050	aŋ tǝ fitha ŋa ka aŋtoŋ ŋa nȧnt , ro kǝkulɔ yi kȧŋȧkŋȧk ɛsek kǝ yi .
40013051	Kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Mȧtȧy ame bɛ mǝ sɔk nu-i ? Aŋ lasi , kaŋ pa , Aŋko , Pa .
40013052	Kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Tiyȧŋ ukarmɔkɔ o karmɔkɔ ɔwe a thǝksa ta rȧbȧy ra ro riyana ɔ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ ulaŋgba ɔwe ba aseth-e , ɔwe mǝ wur ka ɔbɛnɛnɛ wɔŋ yɛt ɛfu yi yɛt ɛkur .
40013053	Ka pǝ re yi ma Yisɔs ɔ po gbanthi ɛlomɔ ɛye-e , ɔ wur ri .
40013054	Ma ɔ der ka ȧŋthɔf ŋɔŋ-e , ɔ thǝksa ŋa ka ȧŋseth ŋaŋ agbanɛ haŋ aŋ kabanɛ , aŋ pa , Reke ɔlaŋgba ɔwe ɔ sɔthɔ kȧtemp ake , dɛ yi mȧyɔs ma afɔsɔ ame-e ?
40013055	Ɔwan ka ɔkamdɛr kɔn tha ɔwe-i ? Ɔwa a bont hɛ ɔkara kɔŋ Meri-i ? Aŋwɔnt ŋɔŋ , ŋa tha yi Yemǝs , Yosef , Saymɔn yi Yudaŋ-i ?
40013056	Ɔwa aŋwɔnt ŋɔŋ abɛra ŋa bɛ aŋ yi hɛ yi saŋ-i ? Reke thɔŋ ɔwuni ɔwe ɔ sɔthɔ mȧtȧy ame bɛ-e ?
40013057	Ka pǝ kɛtha ŋa ta atɔŋ . Kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Unabi ɔ paŋ hɛ ayiki , thambe ka ȧŋthɔf ŋɔŋ gbeŋ , ɔwa ro seth kɔŋ sɔ .
40013058	Tiyȧŋ ɔ yɔ hɛ ri mǝyɔs ma afɔsɔ mǝgbathi salata kate ka ŋaŋ lanɛ .
40014001	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati Herodȧŋ ɔtɛtrark ɔ tǝl tȧgbuŋ ta Yisɔs .
40014002	kɔ pa ka ɛbɔy yɔŋ , Ɔwe-e , Yɔnȧŋ ɔBaftays kɔnɔȧŋ . Ɔ po yokanɛ ka rafi , te ba ti mȧyɔs mǝkabanɛ ame mǝ tɔrinɛ ro ŋɔŋ .
40014003	Ȧtesoma-e Herodȧŋ ɔ po wop Yɔnȧŋ , ɔ sek kɔ , kɔ bot kɔ ka ȧŋseth ŋa tǝrǝŋka salata Herodias , ɔrani ka Filip ɔwɔnt kɔŋ .
40014004	Ȧtesoma-e Yɔn ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Pǝ yi hɛ ɔlompi ta munɔ tǝ kǝba kɔ .
40014005	Ɔwa ma ɔ yema dif kɔ-e , ɔ nesa aŋfǝm , pǝkasifɛ aŋ nanɛ Yɔnȧŋ tǝ kǝyi unabi .
40014006	Kɛrɛ ka amet ma ȧŋrey aŋa a kom Hɛrɔdȧŋ-e , ɔwan ubɛra ka Hɛrɔdiyȧs ɔ thɔmɔ kǝtɔŋ ka ŋaŋ , ka pǝ bɔnɛ Hɛrɔdȧŋ .
40014007	Ta ȧŋsabu ŋati ɔ lahiri rǝ agbiŋ rokɔm tǝ kǝsɔŋ ɔbɔrkɔ koko ɔ thola .
40014008	Kɔnɔŋ , mɔ mǝ ɔya kɔŋ ɔ kanɛ kɔ-e , ɔ pa , Sɔŋ mi nɔ rǝ alɛfa rȧbomp ra Yɔn ɔBaftays .
40014009	Ka pǝ kɛtha ɔbȧy , kɛrɛ salata aŋgbiŋ ŋɔŋ-e , dɛ yi ŋaŋ aŋa yirȧ yi kɔn ka kǝdi-e , ɔ yamari tǝ kǝsɔŋ kɔ ri .
40014010	kɔ som kȧmȧ a gbetha rȧbomp ra Yɔn ka ȧŋseth ŋa tǝrǝŋka .
40014011	Ka a kȧrȧ rȧbomp rɔŋ ka alɛfa , ɔwa a sɔŋ ri ka ɔwath bɛra , kɔ kera ri ka ɔkara kɔŋ .
40014012	Ka aŋkarande ŋa Yɔn aŋ de gbasi kabel , kaŋ maŋk kɔ , kaŋ kɔ kanɛ ti ka Yisɔs .
40014013	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tǝl ti-e , ɔ gbasi abil , kɔ kɔ rǝ dɛr ɔyeŋ . Ma aŋfǝm aŋ tǝl ti-e , aŋ tȧŋ kɔ ro gbaŋ kǝwur ka tapet .
40014014	kɔ wur ka ȧŋbil , ɔ nənk ȧruniya rǝbana , kɔ nǝŋka ŋa ȧney , ɔ damǝr aŋboma ŋaŋ .
40014015	Ɔwa ma rȧfɔy rǝ bek-e , aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ der ro ŋɔŋ , aŋ pa , Ɔdɛr ɔwe ɔ yeŋ , ɔwa ȧŋlɔkɔ aŋ po thɔŋ thas . Ter aŋfǝm aŋ kɔnɛ , kȧmȧ aŋ kɔ ka tagbɔm , aŋ wayanɛ yɛt ɛdi .
40014016	Kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Aŋ ba hɛ tǝ kǝkɔ , sɔŋ ŋa nu yɛt ɛdi .
40014017	kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Sǝ ba gbo anɔ tǝbo tamath dɛ yi ɛlop ŋarǝŋ .
40014018	kɔ pa , Kara yi nɔ ro rɔmi .
40014019	kɔ yamari aŋfǝm kȧmȧ aŋ yirȧ ka akereŋ , kɔ gbasi tabo tamath yi ɛlop ŋarǝŋ , ɔwa ɔ kǝli rokɔm ka ȧkȧriyana , ɔ ruba yi , kɔ simǝth tabo , ɔ sɔŋ ti aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , ka aŋkarande aŋ sɔŋ aŋfǝm .
40014020	Ka ŋa bɛ aŋ di , aŋ namra . Kaŋ gbas ɛbɛm ɛtianɛ aŋ lasǝr tǝbǝlai tɔfɔt tǝrǝŋ .
40014021	Ɔwa ŋaŋ aŋa di-e , aŋ yi mɔlɔ ma afǝm aruni ɛwul tamath kǝte lɔmanɛ bom-ŋaŋ dɛ yi afɛth .
40014022	Ka ɔlɛmp wati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tɔri aŋkarande ŋɔŋ tǝ kǝbaka ka ȧŋbil kȧmȧ aŋ tǝma kɔ kǝdi romɔri , haŋ ɔ po ter aŋfǝm aŋ kɔnɛ .
40014023	Ma ɔ po ter aŋfǝm-e , ɔ gbep ka kateŋ , kɔn son tǝ kǝramnɛ . Ɔwa ma rȧfɔy rǝ bek-e , ɔ yirȧ ri kɔn son .
40014024	Kɛrɛ ȧŋbil aŋ yi thɔŋ ro baŋ ratɔŋ , ka ɛmuŋkǝl ɛ sɔmpa ŋi , kotȧy-e aŋfef aŋ wurǝr ŋa rodi .
40014025	Ma pǝ yema sɔk-e , Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ der ro ŋaŋ , ɔ kɔth ka kȧbȧŋ rokɔm .
40014026	Ma aŋkarande aŋ nənk kɔ mɔ mǝ ɔ kɔth ka kȧbȧŋ rokɔm-e , aŋ nesa , kaŋ pa , Ayina ŋaŋ . Kaŋ sel ɛrɔŋ yi rǝnes .
40014027	Ka ɔlɛmp wati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Bȧk nu tǝbuth ; minɛȧŋ . Te nu nesa .
40014028	Ka Pitarȧŋ ɔ pa , Pa , bepi munɔȧŋ-e , yamari mi i der ro rɔmu ka ȧmȧnt rokɔm .
40014029	kɔ pa , Der . Ka Pitarȧŋ ɔ wur ro bil , ɔ kɔth ka ȧmȧnt rokɔm tǝ kǝder ka Yisɔs .
40014030	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ nənk aŋfef abȧki-e , ɔ nesa . Ɔ tǝp kǝmɔta , kɔ sel ɛrɔŋ ɔ pa , Pa , kisis mi .
40014031	Ka ɔlɛmp wati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ thanthi kȧta kɔŋ , ɔ wop kɔ , ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Munɔ , mun ba kǝlanɛ kǝthan , kɔyɛŋ mǝ sikɛ-e ?
40014032	Ɔwa maŋ po wɔŋ ka ȧŋbil-e , aŋfef aŋ thɔfɔla .
40014033	Ka ŋaŋ aŋa yi ro bil aŋ bȧtho kɔ , aŋ pa , Tɛntɛnɛ munɔ yi ɔWan ka Kuru .
40014034	Maŋ po fǝsi romɔri-e , aŋ bek ka aŋgbaŋ ŋa ro Kɛnɛsarɛt .
40014035	Ma aŋfǝm ŋa ɔdɛr wati aŋ tȧrȧ kɔ-e , aŋ som ka ȧŋthɔf ŋati bɛ , aŋ kȧrȧ ro ŋɔŋ aŋfǝm bɛ aŋa yi atuy .
40014036	kaŋ nɛmthɛnɛ kɔ kȧmȧ aŋ gboŋ hali gbo amɛsɛ ma aruma rɔŋ . Ɔwa ŋaŋ bɛ aŋa gboŋ kɔ-e , aŋ sɔthɔ kǝyeŋk mǝdɛr .
40015001	Ka aŋFarisi yi aŋkarmɔkɔ kǝwur ro Yerusalɛm aŋ der ka Yisɔs , aŋ pa ,
40015002	kɔyɛŋ aŋkarande a mu aŋ lǝsǝr makur ma aŋbȧki ma aŋ te yanɛ yeŋka aŋ di-e ?
40015003	kɔ lasi ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , kɔyɛŋ naŋ sɔ nǝ lǝsǝr aŋyamari ŋa Kuru salata makur ma nu-e ?
40015004	kotȧy-e Kuruȧŋ ɔ pa , Yikis ɔkas ka mu yi ɔkara ka mu , dɛ yi ; Kɔn ɔwe mǝ fɔf ɔlǝs ta ɔkas thalɔm ta ɔkara-e , ta ɔ fi rafi .
40015005	Kɛrɛ naŋ nǝ pa , Wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ pa ka ɔkas kɔŋ thalɔm ɔkara kɔŋ , Arǝka ra mi ara gbǝli naŋ munafas mu-e , a sɔŋ ri Kuru-e ,
40015006	ɔ ba hɛ sɔ tǝ kǝyikis ɔkas kɔŋ thalɔm ɔkara kɔŋ . Ɔwa nǝ po wop ȧrim ra Kuru ɔyai salata makur ma nu .
40015007	Na amunafaki , pǝ yi ɔlompi ȧte ɔnȧbi Isaya ɔ nȧbi ta ȧtȧ nu ma ɔ pa ,
40015008	Aŋfǝm aŋe aŋ yikis mi yi tasǝŋ taŋ , Kɛrɛ ɛmerȧ yaŋ ɛ bɔlȧnɛ mi .
40015009	Kɛrɛ aŋ bȧtho mi gbo kǝtiŋ , aŋ thǝksa ɛmaŋ ya afǝm a kǝpet mɔ mȧthǝksȧ maŋ .
40015010	Mȧ ɔ po tela aŋfǝm ro rɔŋɔŋ-e , ɔ pa , Tǝl nu , ɔwa tȧ pǝ sɔk nu .
40015011	Pǝ yi hɛ arǝka ara mǝ wɔŋ ka kasǝŋ ara mǝ nɔkɔs wuni , kɛrɛ ara mǝ wur ka kasǝŋ , rǝ mǝ nɔkɔs wuni .
40015012	Ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ der kaŋ pa ro rɔŋɔŋ , Mǝ tȧrȧ kǝpa aŋFarisi aŋ bansȧ maŋ tǝl ȧsim ȧte-i ?
40015013	Kɛrɛ ɔ lasi ɔ pa , Ŋǝnt o ŋǝnt aŋa ɔKas kȧmi ro riyana ɔ te tɛp-e , a ba kǝtusi ŋi .
40015014	Tey ŋa , aŋ yi gbo afith aŋa kɔtha aŋfith . Ɔwa bepi ufith ɔ kɔtha ufith-e , ŋa ŋarǝŋ aŋ tǝ fumpɔ ro fo .
40015015	Ka Pita ɔ pa , Lokthia su aŋlomɔ aŋe .
40015016	Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa , Naŋ sɔ nǝ tha ba hɛ kǝsɔthnɛ-i ?
40015017	Nǝ tɛ hɛ kǝpa rǝka o rǝka ara mǝ wɔŋ ro sǝŋ rǝ thas rokor-i , ɔwa a lǝpsɔ fitha ri-i ?
40015018	Kɛrɛ mȧtȧy ama wur ka kasǝŋ mǝ wur ka ȧŋmerȧ ; ɔwa ame-e , mǝ mǝ nɔkɔs wuni .
40015019	Ȧtesoma-e ɛnanɛ ɛlǝs-o , kǝdifǝth-o , kǝrǝp-o , rǝkeiyo , mǝseri ma rǝyem-o yi kǝfɔf Kuru ɔlǝs-e , ɛ wur ka ȧŋmerȧ .
40015020	Mȧtȧy ame mǝ mǝ nɔkɔs wuni , kɛrɛ tǝ kǝdi kǝte yanɛ kǝ nɔkɔs hɛ wuni .
40015021	Ka Yisɔs ɔ wur ri , ɔ kɔ ka ɛgbap ya ro Tair yi ro Sidon .
40015022	Ɔwa wuni bom ka ro Kenan ɔ wur ka ɛgbap yati , ɔ sel ɛrɔŋ ɔ pa , Pa , munɔ ɔwan ka Debid , ba mi ȧney . Ukǝrǝfi ɔ sɔmpa ɔwan kȧmi ubɛra .
40015023	Kɛrɛ ɔ lasianɛ hɛ kɔ hali dim din . Ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ der aŋ nɛmthɛnɛ kɔ , aŋ pa , Yɔ ɔwath ubɛra ɔ kɔnɛ , kotȧy-e ɔ bokǝr su .
40015024	Kɛrɛ ɔ pa , A som mi gbo ka talɔmɛ tǝsɔkar ta ȧŋseth ŋa Isrɛl .
40015025	Ka ɔya ɔ der ɔ sɔna kɔ tǝwu , ɔ pa , Pa , mar mi .
40015026	Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa , Pǝ mar hɛ tǝ kǝgbasi kabo ka aŋfɛth tǝ kǝfitha ki ka ɛtǝn .
40015027	Kɛrɛ ɔwath ubɛra ɔ pa sɔ , Tǝteŋ Pa , kɛrɛ hali ɛtǝn aŋ di atɔmp ȧte mǝ fumpɔ ro thɔf kǝwur ka aŋthebǝl ŋa aŋmarki ŋaŋ .
40015028	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Bithaŋ , kȧlanɛ ka mu kǝ bana . Ta pǝ yɔnɛ mu mɔ mǝ mǝ yema . Ka ɔwan kɔŋ ubɛra ɔ yeŋk ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati gbeŋ .
40015029	Ka Yisɔs ɔ wur ri , ɔ kɔ fatǝr kȧbȧŋ ka ro Kalili . Kɔ gbep ka kateŋ rokɔm , ɔ yirȧ ri .
40015030	Ka suniya tǝbana tǝ der ro ŋɔŋ tǝ banȧnɛ aŋtǝtkɛ-o , aŋfith-o , tabobo-o , aŋlopanɛ-o yi alɔm agbȧthi , ka a bot ŋa ka ȧtȧtək tɔŋ . Kɔ yeŋkǝs ŋa bɛ ,
40015031	haŋ ȧruniya rǝ kabanɛ maŋ nənk tabobo aŋ fɔf , aŋlopanɛ aŋ yeŋk , aŋtǝtkɛ aŋ kɔth yi aŋfith aŋ nənk . Kaŋ yikis ɔKuru ka Isrɛl .
40015032	Ka Yisɔs ɔ tela ro ŋɔŋ aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , ɔ pa , I ba ȧney ta ȧruniya , ȧtesoma-e aŋ po yi yi minɛŋ mǝrei mǝsas , aŋ ba hɛ ra rǝdi . I yema hɛ tey ŋa ŋa ador , ta thani aŋ pika ro roŋ .
40015033	Ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Reke mǝ sǝ sɔthɔ tǝbo tǝgbathi tǝbeki namsǝr ȧruniya rǝbana are ka ɔdɛr ɔyeŋ ɔwe-e ?
40015034	Ka Yisɔs ɔ yif ŋa , Mɔlɔ tǝbo nǝ ba-a ? kaŋ pa , Tamthǝdɛrǝŋ , dɛ yi ɛlop athȧn .
40015035	kɔ kanɛ ȧruniya tǝ kǝyira yirȧ ro thɔf .
40015036	kɔ gbasi tǝbo tamthǝdɛrǝŋ yi ɛlop-e , kɔ muti mɔmɔ , ɔ simǝth yi , kɔ sɔŋ aŋkarande ŋɔŋ kȧmȧ aŋ sɔŋ ȧruniya .
40015037	Ka ŋa bɛ aŋ di aŋ namra , ɔwa aŋ gbas tǝbǝlai tamthǝdɛrǝŋ ka ɛbɛm ɛtianɛ .
40015038	Ɔwa ŋaŋ aŋa di aŋ yi mɔlɔ ma afǝm aruni ɛwul yanlɛ , kǝte lɔmanɛ aŋfǝm abom yi aŋfɛthȧŋ .
40015039	kɔ ter ȧruniya , ɔ bȧkȧ ka ȧŋbil , kɔ der ka ȧŋgbȧp ŋa ro Makadan .
40016001	Ka aŋFarisi yi aŋSadusi aŋ der ro ŋɔŋ tǝ kǝmɛm kɔ , kaŋ yif kɔ tǝ kǝtɔri ŋa amisali kǝwur ro riyana .
40016002	Kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ lasi , ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Ma rȧfɔy rǝ bek-e , nǝ pa , Kǝsalaŋ kǝ tǝ yi ȧtesoma-e ȧkuru kǝ yim .
40016003	Ɔwa , ka rabǝth nǝ pa sɔ-e , Kǝnkǝl kǝ tǝ der thonɔŋ ȧtesoma-e ȧkuru kǝ kuluŋanɛ kǝyim-o yi kǝbiȧŋ . O naŋ amunafaki , nǝ tȧrȧ tǝ kǝgbaski ȧder ra akuru-e , kɛrɛ nǝ tɛ hɛ gbaski ɛmisali ya ɛlɔkɔ .
40016004	Rǝkomra rǝlǝs rǝrǝpi rǝ thɛns ɛmisali , kɛrɛ a ba hɛ kǝsɔŋ ri amisali thambe ȧŋmisali ŋa Yona . Kɔ tey ŋa ɔ kɔnɛ .
40016005	Ma aŋkarande aŋ fǝsi romɔri-e , aŋ pǝnɛ tǝ kǝbananɛ tǝbo .
40016006	Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Botnɛ nu , ɔwa pɛndaf nu ɛgbith ya aŋFarisi yi aŋSadusi .
40016007	kaŋ fɔfǝranɛ , aŋ pa , Sǝ karanɛ hɛ tǝbo .
40016008	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tȧrȧ ti-e , ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , O naŋ nǝ ba kǝlanɛ kǝthan , to som mǝ nǝ fɔfǝranɛ ta ma nǝ te ba tǝbo-e ?
40016009	Pǝ tha sɔk hɛ nu-i , ɔwa nǝ kala hɛ ɛmerȧ ta tabo tamath ta ɛwul tamath , yi amɔlɔ tǝbǝlai nǝ gbasi-i ?
40016010	Thalɔm tabo tamthǝdɛrǝŋ ta ɛwul yanlɛ sɔ , yi amɔlɔ tǝbǝlai nǝ gbasi-i ?
40016011	To som nǝ te tȧrȧ kǝpa i fɔfȧnɛ hɛ nu ta tǝbo-e ? Kɛrɛ pɛndaf nu ta ɛgbith ya aŋFarisi yi aŋSadusi .
40016012	Ka pǝ sɔk ŋa kǝpa ɔ yamari hɛ ŋa tǝ kǝpɛndaf ɛgbith ya tǝbo , kɛrɛ ɔ yamari ŋa ta kathǝksa ka aŋFarisi yi aŋSadusi .
40016013	Ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ bek ka ȧŋgbȧp ŋa ro Sisaria Filipay-e , ɔ yif aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , ƆWan ka wuni , kanɛ aŋfǝm mǝ aŋ pa ɔ yi-e ?
40016014	kaŋ pa , Alɔm aŋ pa Yɔnȧŋ ɔBaftays ; alɔm Ilayaŋ , alɔm Yɛrimayaŋ , thalɔm ukin ka aŋnabi .
40016015	Ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Kɛrɛ naŋ , kanɛ nǝ pa minɛȧŋ i yi-e ?
40016016	Ka Saymɔn Pitarȧŋ ɔ lasi , ɔ pa , Munɔ yi ɔKrayst , ɔWan ka ɔKuru ukǝli .
40016017	Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Munɔ mǝ ba aruba Saymɔn ɔwan ka Yona , pǝkasifɛ wuni kǝpet ɔ tɔri hɛ ti ro mu , kɛrɛ ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40016018	I kȧl sɔ pa ro rɔmu , Munɔ yi Pita , ɔwa rokɔm ka aŋgbalaŋ aŋe rǝ mǝ i tǝmǝr aŋchɔch a mi ; ɔwa tadare ta ro kǝrǝfi tǝ ba hɛ kǝtham ŋi .
40016019	I ti sɔŋ mu mȧsapɔ ma rȧbȧy ra ro riyana , ɔwa koko ara mǝ sek ka ȧdȧru-e a tǝ sek ri ro riyana , dɛ yi koko ara mǝ sǝli ka ȧdȧru-e a tǝ sǝli ri ro riyana .
40016020	kɔ yamari aŋkarande ŋɔŋ kȧmȧ aŋ te tɔri wuni o wuni kǝpa kɔnɔ yi ɔKrayst .
40016021	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ tǝp kǝtɔri aŋkarande ŋɔŋ kǝpa ɔ ba kǝkɔ ro Yerusalɛm tǝ kǝnȧkȧsi mətȧy mǝgbȧthi ka mȧta ma aŋbȧki yi aŋfode ȧbana yi aŋkarmɔkɔ , ɔwa aŋ tǝ dif kɔ , ɔwa ka ȧŋrey aŋa bekȧ mǝsas a tǝ kȧl yokas kɔ .
40016022	Kȧ Pita ɔ kera kɔ rayɛr , kɔ ŋal kɔ , ɔ pa , Ta pǝ bɔlȧnɛ mu Pa . Ȧte tǝ ba hɛ kǝyi mu .
40016023	Kɛrɛ ɔ fǝlɛ , ɔ pa ka Pita , Tɔnɛ mi raŋ Sethani . Mǝ yi mi da rǝpǝnthbǝla ȧtesoma-e munɔ mǝ kǝli hɛ ta mȧtȧy ma Kuru , mǝ kǝli gbo ta mȧtȧy ma afǝm a kǝpet .
40016024	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , Bepi wuni ɔ wuni ɔ yema tȧŋ mi-e , ta ɔ pɛnsanɛ , ɔ gbasi akǝnt kɔŋ kǝpǝŋkinɛ , ɔ tȧŋ mi .
40016025	kotȧy-e wuni o wuni ɔwe yema kisis aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ-e , ɔ tǝ dim ŋi ; ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ dim aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ salata mi ɔ tǝ fir ŋi .
40016026	To mǝ pǝ naŋfas wuni bepi ɔ sɔthɔ ȧdȧru bɛ , kɛrɛ ɔ dim aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ-e ? Thalɔm ko wuni mǝ ɔ gbǝli sɔŋ tǝ kǝsinkar aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ-e ?
40016027	kotȧy-e ɔWan ka wuni ɔ tǝ der ka aŋyiki ŋa ɔKas kɔŋ yi aŋmȧleka ŋɔŋ . Ɔwa ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati ɔ tǝ sɔŋ wuni o wuni amɔlɔ ma mȧyɔs mɔŋ mǝ yi .
40016028	Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , alɔm aŋ tǝma nɔ aŋa te ba kǝnǝŋk rǝfi , haŋ aŋ nənk ɔWan ka wuni ɔ der ka rȧbȧy rɔŋ .
40017001	Ɔwa kǝdarǝŋ ka mǝrei tamthǝrukin-e , Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ keranɛ Pitarȧŋ , Yemǝsȧŋ yi Yɔnȧŋ ɔwɔnt kɔŋ , kɔ gbepa ŋa rǝ kǝteŋ kǝbɔli rǝkɔm , ŋa son .
40017002	Ka rabalanɛ rɔŋ rǝ lafthɛ rodi ka ŋaŋ . Ader rɔŋ rǝ gbɛntha mɔ aret , ɔwa ȧsuma tɔŋ tǝ fera mɔ ɔwaŋ .
40017003	Ɔwa kǝla , Mosisȧŋ yi Ilayaŋ aŋ tɔrinɛ ro ŋaŋ , kaŋ fɔfȧnɛ kɔ .
40017004	Ka Pitȧŋ ɔ pa , Pa , ɔfinɔ ta ȧtȧ su tǝ kǝyi nɔ . Bepi mǝ selɔ-e , i ti bɛmpa nɔ ɛgbɔm ɛsas , ŋin ta ȧtȧ mu , ŋin ta Mosis , dɛ yi ŋin ta Ilaya .
40017005	Ma ɔ yi ka kǝfɔf-e , kǝrǝnt kǝfera kǝgbɛntha kǝ derǝr ŋa ; ɔwa rim rǝ wur ka karǝnt , rǝ pa , ƆWan kȧmi ubɔthǝr kɔnɔ ɔwe , ta ɔwe pǝ thesanɛ mi finɔ . Tǝla kɔ nu .
40017006	Ma aŋkarande aŋ tǝl ti-e , aŋ gbǝpsa , aŋ nesa ɔthasǝr .
40017007	Kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ der ɔ gboŋ ŋa , ɔ pa , Yokanɛ nu , te nu nesa .
40017008	Maŋ ŋata ɛfɔr yaŋ-e , aŋ nənk hɛ wuni o wuni thambe Yisɔsȧŋ son .
40017009	Ɔwa mɔ mǝ aŋ thor ka kateŋ-e , Yisɔs ɔ yamari ŋa , ɔ pa , Te kanɛ wuni o wuni mȧnǝnk ama nǝ po nənk haŋ ɔWan ka wuni ɔ kȧl yokanɛ ka rafi .
40017010	Ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ yif kɔ , aŋ pa , kɔyɛŋ aŋkarmɔkɔ aŋ pa Ilaya ɔ ba kǝmɔtha der-e ?
40017011	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ lasi ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ Ilaya ɔ ba tǝ kǝder , ɔwa ɔ tǝ lompǝs mətȧy bɛ .
40017012	Kɛrɛ i kanɛ nu kǝpa , Ilaya ɔ po thɔŋ der , kɛrɛ aŋ tɛ hɛ kɔ , ɔwa aŋ po yɔ kɔ tȧy o tȧy ȧte aŋ yema . Ɔwa yaŋ sɔ ɔWan ka wuni ɔ tǝ nakasi ka mȧta maŋ .
40017013	Ka pǝ sɔk aŋkarande ŋɔŋ kǝpa ɔ fɔfȧnɛ ŋa ta Yɔn ɔBaftays .
40017014	Maŋ bek ka ȧruniya-e , ulaŋgba ɔ der ro ŋɔŋ , ɔ sɔna kɔ tǝwu , kɔ pa ,
40017015	Pa , ba ȧney ta ɔwan kȧmi uruni , ɔ ba kǝtuk , ɔ sɔmpanɛ ɔbaŋ , kotȧy-e ɛlɔkɔ ɛgbathi ɔ fumpɔ ro nȧnt , ɔwa sɔ-e , ɛlɔkɔ ɛgbathi ɔ fumpɔ ro mȧnt .
40017016	Ka i po kȧrȧ kɔ ka aŋkarande a mu , kɛrɛ aŋ gbǝli hɛ damǝr kɔ .
40017017	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ wosa ɔ pa , O rǝkomra ara te lanɛ , rǝgbolŋanɛ , to mǝ i ba kǝwon yi naŋ-e ? To mǝ i ba kǝwon tǝ kǝmuyu nu-e ? Kara kɔ nɔ ro mi .
40017018	Ka Yisɔs ɔ ŋal ɔkǝrǝfi , kɔ gbapɛ kɔ , ka ɔwath ɔ sɔthɔ kǝyeŋk mǝdɛr ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati gbeŋ .
40017019	Ka aŋkarande aŋ der ka Yisɔs mǝnǝŋkanɛ , aŋ pa , kɔyɛŋ saŋ sǝ te gbǝli wurɔ kɔ-e ?
40017020	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Salata kate lanɛ ka nu . Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , Bepi gbo nǝ ba kǝlanɛ mɔ aluka ŋa amustard nǝ gbǝli pa ka kateŋ ake , Tɔnɛ nɔ mǝ kɔ ro , ɔwa kǝ tǝ tɔnɛ . Ɔwa koko rǝ tui hɛ nu tȧy .
40017021	Kɛrɛ awunɔŋ aŋ wur hɛ thambe rǝ kǝramnɛ yi kǝwop asum .
40017022	Ɔwa maŋ yirȧ ro Kalili-e , Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , A ba kǝlaŋkli ɔWan ka wuni ka mȧta ma aŋfǝm ,
40017023	ɔwa aŋ tǝ dif kɔ , kɛrɛ ka ȧŋrey aŋa bekȧ mǝsas-e , a tǝ yokas kɔ . Ka pǝ nɔsinɛ ŋa ɔthasǝr .
40017024	Maŋ bek ro Kepaniyɔm-e , ŋaŋ aŋa thoŋkla ɛfȧk ya ȧŋseth ŋa Kuru aŋ der ka Pita , kaŋ pa , Ɔkarmɔkɔ ka mu ɔ la hɛ ram ȧdiyɔ ?
40017025	kɔ pa , Aŋko . Ma ɔ wɔŋ ro seth-e yeŋka ɔ fɔf rim-e , Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa , To mǝ nanɛ-e , Saymɔn ? aŋbȧy ŋa ȧdȧru-e ka kanɛ mǝ aŋ sɔthɔ ɛfȧk-e , ka aŋwuth ŋaŋ gbeŋ thalɔm ka atik-e ?
40017026	Ɔwa ma ɔ pa , Ka atik , Yisɔs ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Tiyȧŋ aŋwuth aŋ ba hɛ kǝsɔŋ .
40017027	Kɛrɛ kȧmȧ sǝ te yɔ ŋa aŋ pǝnthbǝla-e , kɔnɛ ro baŋ mǝ fitha anǝmp , liŋ kalop ɔwe mɔtha der . Ma mǝ po kanthi kasǝŋ kɔŋ-e mǝ tǝ fir ri akala . Gbasi ŋi ɔwa sɔŋ ŋa ta ȧtȧ mi yi ta ȧtȧ mu .
40018001	Ka ȧŋlɔkɔ ŋati aŋkarande aŋ der ka Yisɔs , ka aŋ pa , Kanɛ mǝ tha yi ubana bɛ ka rȧbȧy ra ro riana-e ?
40018002	kɔ tela uwath ulɔl ro ŋɔŋ , ɔ tǝmǝr kɔ kǝtɔŋ ka ŋaŋ ,
40018003	kɔ pa , Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , Thambe nǝ lȧfthi ɛmerȧ ɛ nu-e , nǝ sǝkɛ mɔ afɛth alɔl-e , nǝ gbǝli hɛ wɔŋ ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40018004	Tiyȧŋ wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ sanɛ mɔ ɔwath ulɔl ɔwe-e , kɔnɔ tha yi ubana ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40018005	Ɔwa bepi wuni o wuni ɔ malanɛ uwath ulɔl ukin uwunɔŋ ka ȧŋes a mi-e , minɛ ɔ malanɛ .
40018006	Kɛrɛ bepi wuni o wuni ɔ yɔ ukin ka aŋlɔl aŋe aŋa lanɛ mi ɔ pǝnthbǝla-e , pǝ tǝ yi kɔ fisa bepi a gbak kɔ ȧsar ȧgbɔlȧ ȧbana ka kalim kɔŋ , a mɔtas kɔ ka ɔbɔlɔŋ wa kȧbȧŋ .
40018007	Mɔnɛ ka ȧdȧru ta mətȧy mǝpǝnthbǝla , kotȧy-e mȧtȧy mati mǝ ba kǝder ; kɛrɛ mɔnɛ ka ɔwuni kati ɔwe mǝ kȧrȧ ma !
40018008	Tiyȧŋ bepi kȧta ka mu thalɔm akatǝk ka mu kǝ yɔ mu mǝ pǝnthbǝla-e , gbǝk ki , mǝ fitha ki kȧmȧ kǝ bɔlȧnɛ mu . Pǝ tǝ yi mu fisa bepi mǝ wɔŋ ka aŋesǝm mun lopȧnɛ thalɔm mun tǝtkɛ pǝthasi kǝba mǝta mȧrǝŋ thalɔm tatǝk tǝrǝŋ , ɔwa a fitha mu ka anant nǝthǝbana .
40018009	Ɔwa bepi rȧfɔr ra mu rǝ yɔ mu mǝ pǝnthbǝla-e , kothi ri , mǝ fitha ri kȧmȧ rǝ bɔlȧnɛ mu . Pǝ tǝ yi mu fisa bepi mǝ wɔŋ ka aŋesǝm yi rǝfɔr rin-e , pǝthasi kǝba ɛfɔr yɛrǝŋ ɔwa a fitha mu ka anant na ro yahanama .
40018010	Botnɛ nu kȧmȧ nǝ te sai ukin ka aŋlɔl aŋe , kotȧy-e , i kanɛ nu kǝpa ro riyana aŋmȧleka ŋaŋ aŋ kǝli lɔkɔ o lɔkɔ ȧder ra ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riyana .
40018011	Ȧtesoma-e ɔWan ka wuni ɔ der tǝ kǝkisis aŋa po dinɛ .
40018012	To nǝ nanɛ-e ? Bepi wuni ɔ ba tǝlɔmɛ kɛmɛ kin , ɔwa ukin ka ŋaŋ ɔ sɔkar-e , ɔ tey hɛ antǝgba tanlɛ tɔfɔt tamthǝrɛŋanlɛ , ɔ kɔnɛ ka tȧteŋ tǝ kǝthɛns ɔwe sɔkar-i ?
40018013	Ɔwa bepi pǝ yi ɔ fir kɔ-e , i kanɛ nu tɛntɛnɛ ɔ tǝ selǝr kɔ mǝbɔnɛ pǝthasi ta antǝgba tanlɛ tɔfɔt tamthǝrɛŋanlɛ aŋa te sɔkar .
40018014	Ya pǝ yi sɔ-e , pǝ yi hɛ mȧselɔ ma ɔKas ka nu ɔwe yi ro riyana kȧmȧ ukin ka aŋlɔl aŋe ɔ dinɛ .
40018015	Ɔwa bepi ɔwɔnt mu ɔ yɔ mu ɔlǝs-e , kɔ tɔri kɔ ɔlǝs wɔŋ na ŋarǝŋ son ; bepi ɔ sua mu ɛlǝns-e , mǝ po sɔthɔ ɔwɔnt mu ,
40018016	kɛrɛ bepi ɔ sua hɛ mu ɛlǝns-e , banȧnɛ wuni kin thalɔm ŋarǝŋ kȧmȧ ka tasǝŋ ta mǝseri ŋarǝŋ thalɔm asas-e , rim o rim rǝ tǝma .
40018017	Ɔwa bepi ɔ kasi kǝsuwa ŋa ɛlǝns-e , kanɛ ti ka aŋchɔch . Bepi ɔ selɔ hɛ sua ɛlǝns ka aŋchɔch-e , ta ɔ yi ro mu mɔ wuni tel dɛ yi ugbasi ɛfȧk .
40018018	Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , rǝka o rǝka ara mǝ nǝ sek nɔru rǝ tǝ yi rǝsek ro riyana , ɔwa rǝka o rǝka ara mǝ nǝ sǝli ka ȧdȧru-e rǝ tǝ yi rǝsǝli ro riyana .
40018019	I kanɛ nu sɔ , bepi ŋarǝŋ kǝtɔŋ ka nu aŋ ba dim din ka ȧdȧru ta tȧy o tȧy ȧtȧ mǝ nǝ yif-e , ɔKas kȧmi ɔwe yi ro riyana ɔ tǝ yɔna nu ti .
40018020	kotȧy-e , ro ŋarǝŋ thalɔm asas-e mǝ aŋ gbanɛ dɛr rɔkin ka ȧŋes a mi-e , rǝ i yi kǝtɔŋ ka ŋaŋ .
40018021	Ka Pitarȧŋ ɔ der ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Mariki , amɔlɔ ɔwɔnt mi mǝ ɔ yɔ mi ɔlǝs , ɔwa i tera kɔ-a ? Haŋ kǝtǝma tamthǝdɛrǝŋ-a ?
40018022	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ wosa ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , I pa hɛ ro mu haŋ tamthǝdɛrǝŋ , kɛrɛ haŋ ɛlɔkɔ tǝgba tǝsas tɔfɔt kǝtǝma tamthǝdɛrǝŋ .
40018023	Tiyȧŋ rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ ubȧy ulɔm ɔwe yema lɔmǝsnɛ yi ɛbɔy yɔŋ .
40018024	Ma ɔ tǝp kǝlɔmǝs-e , a kȧrȧ ukin ro ŋɔŋ ɔwe ba kǝram kɔ ɛtalent ɛwul tɔfɔt .
40018025	Kɛrɛ ma ɔ te ba rǝka tǝ kǝrȧm-e , ɔmarki kɔŋ ɔ yamari kȧmȧ a thila kɔ , ɔrani kɔŋ-o , aŋwuth ŋɔŋ-o yi ara ɔ ba bɛ kȧmȧ ȧŋrȧm aŋ wur .
40018026	Tiyȧŋ ȧŋbɔy ɔ gbǝpsa , kɔ nɛmthɛnɛ kɔ , ɔ pa , Pa , muyu mi ɔwa i ti po ram mu bɛ .
40018027	Ka ȧney aŋ wop ɔmarki ka ȧŋbɔy ŋati , kɔ ter kɔ , ɔ tera kɔ sɔ rabei .
40018028	Kɛrɛ ȧŋbɔy ukin kati ɔ wur , kɔ fir ɔkos kɔŋ ȧbɔy ɔwe ba kǝram kɔ ɛsiliŋ kɛmɛ kin . Kɔ wop kɔ , ɔ tɔker kɔ ro bolo , ɔ pa , Ram mi ara mǝ ba kǝram mi .
40018029	Ka ɔkos kɔŋ ȧbɔy ɔ gbǝpsa ɔ nɛmthɛnɛ , kɔ pa , Muyu mi , ɔwa i ti ram mu .
40018030	Kɛrɛ ɔ selɔ hɛ , ɔ kɔ bot kɔ ka ȧŋseth ŋa tǝrǝŋka haŋ ɔ ram rabei rɔŋ .
40018031	Ma aŋkos ŋɔŋ ɛbɔy aŋ nənk ȧte po yɔnɛ-e , ȧney ȧbana aŋ wop ŋa , kaŋ der aŋ der aŋ tɔri ɔmarki ka ŋaŋ ȧte yɔnɛ bɛ .
40018032	Ka ɔmarki kɔŋ ɔ tela kɔ ro ŋɔŋ , ɔ pa , Munɔ , mun ȧbɔy ulǝs , i tera mu rȧbȧy araŋ bɛ , pǝkasifɛ mɔ nɛmthɛnɛ mi .
40018033	Munɔ , mǝ gbǝli hɛ sɔ ba ȧney ta ɔkos mu ȧbɔy-i , mɔ minɛȧŋ i ba mu ȧney-i ?
40018034	Ka ɔmarki kɔŋ ɔ bansȧ , kɔ lȧnki kɔ kia aŋa mǝ thalǝr afǝm haŋ ɔ po ram bɛ ara ɔ ba tǝ kǝram .
40018035	Ya ɔKas kȧmi ro riyana mǝ ɔ yɔ nu sɔ bepi naŋ bɛ nǝ tera hɛ wuni o wuni ɔwɔnt kɔŋ ka ɛmerȧ ɛ nu .
40019001	Ka pǝ re yi ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ gbanthi ȧsim ȧte-e , ɔ wur ro Kalili , ɔ der ka ȧŋgbȧp ŋa ro Yudia aŋa yi ro Yɔrdan mɔri .
40019002	Ka suniya tǝbana tǝ tȧŋ kɔ , kɔ yeŋkǝs ŋa ri .
40019003	AŋFarisi sɔ aŋ der ro ŋɔŋ , kȧmȧ aŋ gbɔns kɔ , kaŋ pa , Pǝ yi ɔlompi ta wan duni tǝ kǝter ɔrani kɔŋ ta tȧy o tai-i ?
40019004	kɔ wosa ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Nǝ tha karaŋ hɛ kǝpa kɔnɔ ɔwe bɛmpa ŋa kǝbi ka ɔtǝpɛr ɔ bɛmpa ŋa uruni dɛ yi ubɛra-i ?
40019005	kɔ pa , Ta ȧŋsabu aŋe wan duni mǝ ɔ tey ɔkas kɔŋ yi ɔkara kɔŋ , ɔ gbapsa ɔrani kɔŋ ; ɔwa ŋa ŋarǝŋȧŋ aŋ sǝkɛ adɛr ŋin-i ?
40019006	Tiyȧŋ aŋ yi hɛ sɔ ŋarǝŋ kɛrɛ ukin . Ɔwa ȧrȧ Kuru ɔ po tɔsa der ɔkin-e , tȧ wuni ɔ te ri tɔsi .
40019007	kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , kɔyɛŋ mǝn Mosis ɔ yamari tǝ kǝsɔŋ areka ŋa kǝsakanɛ dɛ yi tǝ kǝter kɔ-e ?
40019008	kɔ pa ro rɔŋaŋ , Ta salata kabak ka nu ɛmerȧ Mosis ɔ selɔ nu tǝ kǝter aŋrani a nu , kɛrɛ ka katǝp pǝ yi hɛ yaŋ .
40019009	Ɔwa i kanɛ nu , wuni o wuni ɔwe mǝ ter ɔrani kɔŋ , thambe ta ȧŋsabu ŋa kǝrǝp , ɔ kȧl nȧntȧ ulɔm-e , ɔ yɔ kǝrǝp . Kɔnɔ sɔ ɔwe mǝ nȧntȧ ɔbɛra ɔwe a ter-e , ɔ yɔ kǝrǝp .
40019010	Ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Bepi ya pǝ yi kǝtɔŋ ka ɔwan duni yi ɔrani kɔŋ-e , pǝ tǝ yi naŋ fisa tǝ kǝte nȧntȧ .
40019011	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Afǝm bɛ tha mǝ gbǝli malanɛ ȧŋpa aŋe , thambe ŋaŋ ka aŋa a sɔŋ ŋi .
40019012	kotȧy-e afǝm agbȧy aŋ yi aŋa a kom yaŋ kǝbi ka ator ta aŋkara ŋaŋ ; afǝm agbȧy alɔm aŋ yi aŋa afǝm a kǝpet aŋ gbai ; ɔwa alɔm aŋ yi aŋa sǝkinɛ agbȧy salata rȧbȧy ra ro riyana . Kɔnɔ ɔwe gbǝli wop ti ta ɔ wop ti .
40019013	Ka a kȧrȧ afɛth ka Yisɔs kȧmȧ ɔ reŋ mȧta mɔŋ ro ŋaŋ , ɔ ramnɛ ; kɛrɛ aŋkarande aŋ ŋal ŋa .
40019014	Kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa , Ter aŋfɛth kȧmȧ aŋ der ro mi , te nu bɛnt ŋa , kotȧy-e , awunɔŋ ŋa ba rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40019015	kɔ reŋ ŋa mȧta mɔŋ , kɔ wur ri ɔ kɔnɛ .
40019016	Ɔwa kǝla , wuni kin ɔ der ro ŋɔŋ , kɔ pa , Karmɔkɔ , ko tȧy tǝfinɔ tǝ mǝ i yɔ kȧmȧ i sɔthɔ aŋesǝm thǝbana-e ?
40019017	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa , kɔyɛŋ mǝ mǝ bont mi ufinɔ-e ? Ukin gbo kɔnɔ yi ufinɔ , kɔnɔ yi mɔ Kuruȧŋ . Kɛrɛ bepi mǝ yema wɔŋ ka aŋesǝm , wop ɛthɔ .
40019018	kɔ yif kɔ , Ɛreke-e ? Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa , Te dif , te yɔ kǝrǝp , te keya , te sɔŋ mǝseri ma rǝyem .
40019019	Yikis ɔkas ka mu yi ɔkara ka mu , ɔwa mǝ yi tǝ kǝbɔthǝr ɔfatanɛ ka mu mɔ mǝ bɔthǝrnɛ .
40019020	Ka ɔlaŋgba ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Mȧtȧy ame bɛ i po wop kǝbi ka rafɛth ra mi . Ko i paŋ ras-e ?
40019021	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Bepi mǝ yema yi ugbenthis-e , kɔnɛ mǝ thila ara mǝ ba , ɔwa mǝ sɔŋ ȧŋmɔnɛ . Mǝ tǝ ba kɛŋ ro riyana , ɔwa der , mǝ tȧŋ mi .
40019022	Kɛrɛ ma ɔlaŋgba ɔ tǝl ȧsim ȧte ɔ kɔnɛ yi ɔnɔsinɛ , ȧtesoma-e ɔ ba yɛt ɛgbathi .
40019023	Ka Yisɔs ɔ pa ka aŋkarande ŋɔŋ , Tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu , tȧy tǝbaki mǝdɛr tȧŋ ta uyola tǝ kǝwɔŋ ka rȧbȧy ra ro riyana .
40019024	I kanɛ nu sɔ , tȧy tǝyai tȧŋ ta ȧyɔkmɛ tǝ kǝsɔnthɔs rafɔr ra ȧŋsɛni , pǝthasi uyola tǝ kǝwɔŋ ka rȧbȧy ra Kuru .
40019025	Ma aŋkarande ŋɔŋ aŋ tǝl ti-e , aŋ kabanɛ ɔthasǝr , kaŋ pa , Kanɛ thɔŋ mǝ gbǝli kisi-e ?
40019026	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ kǝli ŋa tǝŋ , kɔ pa , Ka afǝm aŋfɔsɔ ŋati aŋ yi hɛ , kɛrɛ ka Kuru aŋfɔsɔ ŋati bɛ aŋ yi .
40019027	Ka Pitarȧŋ ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Kǝla , saŋ sǝ po tey bɛ kȧmȧ sǝ tȧŋ mu ; tiyȧŋ ko ȧrȧm ŋaŋ mǝ sǝ sɔthɔ-e ?
40019028	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ pa , Tǝ tɛntɛnɛ i kanɛ nu-e , ka ȧdȧru rǝfu ma ɔWan ka wuni mǝ ɔ yirȧ ka kawaŋ ka rȧbȧy ka aŋyiki ŋɔŋ-e , naŋ aŋa po tȧŋ mi , naŋ sɔ nǝ tǝ yirȧ ka tǝwaŋ ta rȧbȧy tɔfɔt tǝrǝŋ , nǝ tǝ thonkas ɛbɔnsɔŋ tɔfɔt yɛrǝŋ ya aŋIsrɛl ,
40019029	Ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe po tey ɛseth , thalɔm awɔnt aruni , thalɔm awɔnt abɛra , thalɔm ukas , thalɔm ukara , thalɔm urani , thalɔm awuth , thalɔm tǝthɔf salata ȧŋes a mi-e , ɔ tǝ bȧr sɔthɔ mɔlɔ ma kǝtǝma kɛmɛ kin , ɔwa ɔ tǝ sɔthɔ sɔ aŋesǝm thǝbana .
40019030	Kɛrɛ agbȧthi aŋa yi ȧtɔtɔkɔ aŋ tǝ yi alǝpsɔ . Ɔwa aŋa yi alǝpsɔ aŋ tǝ yi ȧtɔtɔkɔ .
40020001	Ȧtesoma-e rȧbȧy ra ro riyana rǝ bȧlȧnɛ mɔ wuni ɔwe ba kǝfus , kɔ wur bǝth bǝth tǝ kǝyamɔ afǝm tǝ kǝyɔ mǝpanth ka akɔr kɔŋ ka yɛt ɛtɛp ɛgbam .
40020002	Ma ɔ po gbanɛ mɔlɔ yi aŋyɔ mǝpanth ta asiliŋ ta arey ŋin-e , ɔ som ŋa ka akɔr kɔŋ .
40020003	Ma ɔ wur ka aŋhawa aŋa bekȧ mǝsas-e , ɔ nənk alɔm aŋ tǝma ka ɔdɛr ɔthila kǝte ba mǝpanth .
40020004	kɔ pa ro rɔŋaŋ , Naŋ sɔ-e , kɔ nu ka mapanth ro kɔr , ɔwa i ti sɔŋ nu ara yi rǝlompi . Kaŋ kɔnɛ .
40020005	kɔ wur sɔ ka aŋhawa aŋa bekȧ tamthǝrukin yi tamthǝrɛŋanlɛ , kɔ yɔ yi sɔ .
40020006	Ka aŋhawa aŋa bekȧ tɔfɔt ŋin , ɔ wur sɔ-e , kɔ bǝp alɔm aŋ tǝma tǝma gbo , ɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , kɔyɛŋ mǝ nǝ tǝma nɔ pali nǝ te yɔ mǝpanth-e ?
40020007	kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Pǝkasifɛ wuni o wuni ɔ tha yamɔ hɛ su . Kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Kɔnɛ nu sɔ ro kɔr , ɔwa ara yi rǝlompi , rǝ i ti sɔŋ nu .
40020008	Ɔwa ma rȧfɔy rǝ bek-e , ɔmarki ka akɔr ɔ pa ka ȧŋbɔy ŋɔŋ ubaki , Tela aŋyɔ mǝpanth , mǝ ram ŋa aŋkala ŋaŋ , mǝ tǝp ka ɔlǝpsɔ mǝ gbanthi ka ɔtɔtɔkɔ .
40020009	Ka ŋaŋ aŋa lǝpsɔ wɔŋ ka mapanth aŋ der , aŋ sɔthɔ ukin o kin asiliŋ .
40020010	Ma aŋtɔtɔkɔ aŋ der-e , aŋ nanɛ kǝpa a tǝ bȧrȧ ŋa , kɛrɛ ŋaŋ sɔ aŋ sɔthɔ ukin o kin asiliŋ .
40020011	Maŋ wop ŋi-e , aŋ fɔfthənɛ ta ɔwe yamɔ ŋa ,
40020012	aŋ pa , Aŋe-e , ŋa lǝpsɔ wɔŋ ka mapanth , aŋ bulɔ gbo ahawa ŋin . Ɔwa mǝ po yɔ ŋa aŋ thǝnanɛ yi saŋ-e , saŋ aŋa thɔrɔ ɔlel ka ɔwon wa ȧŋrey .
40020013	Kɛrɛ ɔ wosa , ɔ pa ka ukin ka ŋaŋ , Yathki , i yɔ hɛ mu ɔlǝs . Sǝ gbanɛ hɛ yi munɔ ta asiliŋ-i ?
40020014	Gbasi ara yi ara mu , mǝ kɔnɛ . Mȧselɔ ma mi miyɛŋ tǝ kǝsɔŋ aŋlǝpsɔ aŋe mɔ mǝ i po sɔŋ mu .
40020015	Pǝ lomp hɛ ta ȧtȧ mi tǝ kǝyɔ mɔ mǝ i yema yi akɛŋ ka mi-i ? thalɔm mǝ ba kǝtut ta mafinɔ ma mi-i ?
40020016	Tiyȧŋ aŋlǝpsɔ aŋ tǝ yi ȧtɔtɔkɔ ɔwa aŋtɔtɔkɔ aŋ tǝ yi alǝpsɔ . Kotȧy-e a tela agbȧthi , kɛrɛ a thith athȧn .
40020017	Ɔwa ma Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ bɔ kɔ ro Yerusalɛm-e , ɔ gbasi aŋkarande tɔfɔt ŋarǝŋ rayɛr ka aroŋ , kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ ,
40020018	Ɔwa sǝ kɔ ro Yerusalɛm . A tǝ lȧnki ɔWan ka wuni ka aŋfode ȧbana yi aŋkarmɔkɔ ɔwa a tǝ sɔŋ kɔ mǝtheri tǝ kǝfi .
40020019	Aŋ tǝ lȧnki kɔ ka tȧbona tǝlɔm kȧmȧ aŋ sel kɔ , ɔwa aŋ tǝ sap kɔ , aŋ tǝ tȧŋ kɔ ka kǝnt kǝpǝŋkinɛ . Ɔwa ka ȧŋrey aŋa bekȧ mǝsas-e , ɔ tǝ yokanɛ .
40020020	Ka ɔkara ka aŋwuth ŋa Sɛbidi ɔ der ka Yisɔs yi aŋwuth ŋɔŋ aruni , kaŋ bȧtho kɔ , kɔ tholir kɔ tȧy .
40020021	kɔ pa ka ɔya , Ko mǝ yema-e ? Ka ɔya ɔ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Yamari kȧmȧ aŋwuth a mi aruni ŋarǝŋ aŋe aŋ yirȧ , ukin ka kȧdiyɔ ka mu , ɔwa ukin ka kȧmɛrɔ ka mu ka rȧbȧy ra mu .
40020022	Kɛrɛ Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ wosa ɔ pa , Nǝ tɛ hɛ ȧte nǝ yif . Nǝ gbǝli mun ka ampɔthi mǝ i re mun-i ? A gbǝli baftays nu yi ȧŋbaftisəm aŋa a baftays mi-i ? kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Sǝ gbǝli .
40020023	kɔ pa ro ŋaŋ , Tɛntɛnɛ nǝ tǝ mun ka ampɔthi a mi , ɔwa a tǝ baftays nu yi ȧŋbaftisəm aŋa a baftays mi . Kɛrɛ tǝ kǝyira ka kȧdiyɔ kȧmi yi ka kȧmɛrɔ ka mi-e , tȧy ta mi tǝ kǝsɔŋ thahɔ , kɛrɛ a tǝ sɔŋ ti ka ŋaŋ ta aŋa ɔKas kȧmi ɔ bɛnɛ ti .
40020024	Ma aŋtɔfɔt aŋ tǝl ti-e , pǝ bansȧnɛ ŋa ta aŋwɔnt ŋarǝŋ .
40020025	Kɛrɛ Yisɔs ɔ tela ŋa ro ŋɔŋ , kɔ pa , Nǝ tȧrȧ kǝpa aŋbȧki ŋa tȧbona tǝlɔm aŋ gbǝka ŋa , ɔwa aŋfǝm ŋaŋ ȧbana aŋ yɔ ŋa afɔsɔ .
40020026	Kɛrɛ ya tha mǝ pǝ yi kǝtɔŋ ka nu . Wuni o wuni ɔwe yema yi ubana kǝtɔŋ ka nu , ta ɔ yi ȧbɔy a nu .
40020027	Ɔwa wuni o wuni ɔwe yema yi utɔtɔkɔ , ta ɔ yi utar ka nu ;
40020028	mɔ mǝ ɔWan ka wuni ɔ te der kȧmȧ a yɔna kɔ , kɛrɛ tǝ kǝyɔna afǝm , dɛ yi tǝ kǝsɔnd aŋesǝm ŋɔŋ tǝ kǝbani afǝm alai .
40020029	Maŋ wur kǝyɛfǝ ro Yɛriko-e , runiya rǝbana rǝ tȧŋ kɔ .
40020030	Ɔwa afǝm afith ŋarǝŋ aŋ yirȧ ro roŋ rayɛr , ma aŋ tǝl kǝpa Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ thas-e , aŋ sel ɛrɔŋ , aŋ pa , Pa , ba su ȧney , munɔ ɔwan ka Debid .
40020031	Ka ȧruniya rǝ ŋal ŋa kȧmȧ aŋ taŋk , kɛrɛ aŋ bȧr sel ɛrɔŋ , aŋ pa , Pa , ba su ȧney , munɔ ɔwan ka Debid .
40020032	Ka Yisɔs ɔ tǝma son , ɔ tela ŋa ɔ pa , Ko nǝ yema i yɔna nu-e ?
40020033	kaŋ pa ro ŋɔŋ , Pa , kȧmȧ a kanthi ɛfɔr ɛ su .
40020034	Ka Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ ba ŋa ȧney , ɔ gboŋ ɛfɔr yaŋ . Ɔwa ka ɔlɛmp wati aŋ sɔthɔ kakǝli ka ŋaŋ , kaŋ tȧŋ kɔ .
40021001	Maŋ fatǝr ro Yerusalɛm-e , ɔwa aŋ bek ro Bɛthfeki ka kateŋ ka Ɔlif-e , Yisɔsȧŋ ɔ som aŋkarande ŋarǝŋ ,
40021002	ɔ pa ro rɔŋaŋ , Kɔ nu ka kagbɔm ȧke lomanɛ nu , ɔwa nǝ tǝ bǝp ri asofali ukotǝr , yi ɔwan kɔŋ ufɛth . Sǝli ŋa nu kȧmȧ nǝ kȧrȧ ŋa ro mi .
40021003	Bepi wuni o wuni ɔ pa rim ro rɔnu , pa nu , ƆMariki kɔnɔ yema ŋa , kɛrɛ ɔ tǝ kȧl somra ŋa .
40021004	Ȧte bɛ tǝ po yi kȧmȧ ȧrim ra ɔnȧbi rǝ lasǝr ara pa ,
40021005	Kanɛ nu ɔwan ubɛra ka ro Sayɔn , Kǝli ɔbȧy ka mu ɔ der ro rɔmu , Uthɔfǝl bɛm , ɔ rensa asofali , Asofali ufɛth .
40021006	Ka aŋkarande aŋ kɔnɛ , aŋ yɔ mɔ mǝ Yisɔs ɔ kanɛ ŋa ,
40021007	kaŋ kȧrȧ aŋsofali yi ɔwan kɔŋ ufɛth , kaŋ reŋ ŋa ȧsuma taŋ , kɔ yirȧ rokɔm kati ,
40021008	Ka agbȧthi ka ȧruniya aŋ rɛn ȧsuma taŋ ro roŋ . Alɔm aŋ gbǝk mara ka ɛyint-e , kaŋ rɛn ma ro roŋ .
40021009	Ka ȧsuniya ȧte yi kɔ rodi yi ŋaŋ aŋa tȧŋ kɔ , aŋ sel ɛrɔŋ , kaŋ pa , Hosana ka ɔwan ka Debid . Uruba wɔŋ ɔwe der ka ȧŋes ŋa ɔMarki , Hosana ka rokɔm kɔm bɛ !
40021010	Ma ɔ po bek ro Yerusalɛm-e , kȧpet bɛ kǝ yagba , kǝ pa , Kanɛ ɔwe-e ?
40021011	Ka ȧsuniya tǝ pa , Yisɔsȧŋ , ɔnȧbi ka ro Nasarɛth ake ro Kalili , kɔnɔȧŋ .
